# Update from Ella 6.0 to a higher version | Ella Documentation

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#things-to-know-before-you-update-the-theme)

Things to know before you update the theme:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

The Logic of Updating a theme in Shopify platform:

*   Ella is the same as any other Shopify themes in Shopify platform. That is when a new update version released, it will be a core theme source, independent from the previous ones you are using. Thus, your changes on the previous versions will not be included in the update.
    
*   To update the theme to the latest version, you can follow our next instructions. We will guide you how to update theme and help you save your settings.
    
*   Any custom works/ customizations/ changes which are not available from theme core default will be lost and needs customization from the starting point.
    

circle-info

**Remember:** The instructions below are applied to update the theme without losing default settings in Theme Editor **(Not including the customization and app's code). All custom works which were changed in our theme files** **will not be updated** **and have to be redone manually.**

About the apps you installed, you might need to install them again. We recommend you contact the app provider to have support because we're not able to handle the app's code.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#starting-your-update)

Starting your update:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your store is using from **Ella 6.0 version** and you would like to update to the latest version, please follow below instruction:

Instruction Video

circle-info

You should duplicate your current theme to avoid issues (if any) when updating the theme.

1.  Go to your account on **Themeforest** to download the latest theme source.
    
2.  Upload the latest theme source into your store.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FdiTF3IhJ5dpAglqTHvoL%252F142.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a763e0c-8662-42f9-9c18-eb53617c6239&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=830dd2d8&sv=2)

There are some files that need to be copied to maintain your modifications in the latest theme source

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-01-update-for-theme-settings)

**01: Update for Theme Settings:**

1.  Go to the old theme source -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **settings\_data.json** and **COPY ALL** codes.
    
2.  Go to the new theme source which you just installed into your site -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **settings\_data.json**, **delete and PASTE codes you just copied into this file.**
    

circle-info

At this step, you can get some errors because of header and footer in section groups, follow this video to fix: [https://youtu.be/zM4oGyxOSDsarrow-up-right](https://youtu.be/zM4oGyxOSDs)
 (Read our video description for the explanation about why the errors appear when updating to version 6.5.0) Our support team is available to support you if you need our help: [https://halosoft.ticksy.com/arrow-up-right](https://halosoft.ticksy.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-02-update-for-home-page)

**02: Update for Home Page:**

1.  Go to the old theme source -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **index.json** and **COPY ALL** codes.
    
2.  Go to the new theme source which you just installed into your site -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **index.json**, **delete and PASTE codes you just copied into this file.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-03-update-for-header)

**03: Update for Header:**

circle-info

From Ella versions 6.0.0 to less than 6.5.0, skip this instruction as the header-group.json does not exist in your current theme source. [Follow the alternative instruction](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop)
 to set up the header.

From Ella 6.5.0 to the latest version, we have updated the Header to Header Group. Follow the instruction below to maintain the same header layout in the newest theme source.

1.  Go to the old theme source -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **header-group.json** and **COPY ALL** codes.
    
2.  Go to the new theme source which you just installed into your site -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **header-group.json**, **delete and PASTE codes you just copied into this file.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-04-update-for-footer)

**04: Update for Footer:**

circle-info

From Ella versions 6.0.0 to less than 6.5.0, skip this instruction as the footer-group.json does not exist in your current theme source. [Follow the alternative instruction](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout)
 to set up the header.

From Ella 6.5.0 to the latest version, we have updated the Footer to Footer Group. Follow the instruction below to maintain the same header layout in the newest theme source.

1.  Go to the old theme source -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **footer-group.json** and **COPY ALL** codes.
    
2.  Go to the new theme source which you just installed into your site -> **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **footer-group.json**, **delete and PASTE codes you just copied into this file.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-05-update-for-other-pages)

**05: Update for other Pages:**

circle-info

Repeat the procedure: Copy codes in file from old theme source, go to the corresponding file in new theme source, **delete and PASTE codes you just copied** for other pages:

*   Collection List Page => **list-collections.json**
    
*   Collection Page => **collection.json**
    
*   Product Page => **product.json**
    
*   Blog Page => **blog.json**
    
*   Blog Detail Page => **article.json**
    
*   For Inner pages such as: About us, Contact us... => Search "**page.template**" to see the corresponding files
    

For any other pages you have created yourself, they are not included in the newer theme sources.

To keep the same layout + settings of pages, please go to **Edit Code** -> **Templates** -> Search **.json** to see all files of page template.

**Copy codes in file** from the old theme source, go to the corresponding file in new theme source, **delete and PASTE codes you just copied.**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fy6uETnSoLCs23HaPWY8P%252Fupdate.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80d31059-ff12-4ef7-beb9-05ed94b18562&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c40d91a8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-06-update-for-language-files)

**06: Update for Language files:**

1.  Go to the old theme source -> **Edit Code** **\->** **Locales**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FndusknRZVjwwWFfdQJK1%252FScreenshot_2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4f58949-7d20-4657-b1e6-bd1b743b4053&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b2b1b6f&sv=2)

2\. Open the file of your languages. Example we are using German, we will open **de.json** file

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FpSQHLnXNVRIeI9xpyFuH%252FScreenshot_3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De86fc7ba-37c2-4acb-b4e9-c7ffbd5753af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26145ad5&sv=2)

3\. **Copy** all codes in the language file from **the old theme source** and go to the corresponding language file in new theme source, **delete and PASTE codes you just copied.**

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-07-update-custom-css--custom-js)

07: Update Custom CSS + Custom JS

triangle-exclamation

Note:

*   This instruction only applies in case **you (yourself)** make any changes, custom code/ customizations in these 2 files: **custom.css** or **custom.js**
    
*   If you make changes not only on these 2 files, but also on other files (such as liquid, Json), you have to do by yourself again.
    

**If you don't make any changes in these 2 files, please skip this instruction below.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-01-custom-css)

**01: Custom CSS**

**Step 1: Copy CSS from the custom.css file:**

1.  Select the theme source with previous version before updating.
    
2.  Go to **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **custom.css** and **COPY ALL.**
    

**Step 2: Paste CSS to the custom.css file:**

1.  Select the newest theme source after updating.
    
2.  Go to **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **custom.css**, **delete and PASTE code you just copied into this file.**
    
3.  Click **Save.**
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#id-02-custom-js)

**02: Custom JS**

**Step 1: Copy JS from the custom.js file:**

1.  Select the theme source with previous version before updating.
    
2.  Go to **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **custom.js** and **COPY ALL.**
    

**Step 2: Paste JS to the custom.js file:**

1.  Select the newest theme source after updating.
    
2.  Go to **Edit Code** **\->** Open this file **custom.js**, **delete and PASTE code you just copied into this file.**
    
3.  Click **Save.**
    

**\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\*\***

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/update-theme/update-from-ella-6.0-to-a-higher-version#theme-update-service)

# Wishlist | Ella Documentation

A wish list allows shoppers to create personalized collections of products they want to buy and send them to their mail for future reference.

circle-info

Customers don't need to log in to the site to create the wish list. The store owner can't know the wish list of customers unless customers send an email to the store owner.

The wish list is saved until customers clear cache or reinstall the browser.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Wishlist**.
    

Settings

Meaning

Enable wishlist

Enable wishlist feature on your website.

Show wishlist count in mobile menu

Display wishlist count on mobile.

Page link

Specify the page where you want to apply the wishlist template.

circle-info

By default, Wishlist will be enabled, but to make wishlist work, you need to [create a wishlist page](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/page/wishlist-page)
.

[PreviousFaviconchevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general/favicon)
[NextX-shaped cursorchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general/x-shaped-cursor)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Lazy load image | Ella Documentation

The **Lazy Load Image** feature enhances website performance by loading images only as they come into view. This reduces initial load time and conserves bandwidth, providing a smoother browsing experience for users.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme Settings -> General -> Lazy load image**.
    

Setting

Description

Enable lazy load image

Enable lazy load image feature on your website.

[NextSlider dotschevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general/slider-dots)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Swatch | Ella Documentation

Enter the product option name into the box "**Option name**" to show color swatch style for that option. Color swatch style is usually applied for **Color** option to show normal colors or get a custom image for special color or get product images for each variant from product admin. [Follow this instruction for more detailed](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-variant)

circle-info

Please note that for the basic color setup (use variant image), if the variant hasn't been set with any image, the swatch type will fall back to use variant's color name.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Swatch**.
    

**Swatch**

Setting

Description

Width

Determines the width of the swatch options.

Height

Determines the height of the swatch options.

Corner radius

Set the radius of the swatch's corners. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 1px (pixel).

**Color swatch**

Setting

Description

Option Name

Enter the name of the option you want to display as a color swatch.

Example: **Color**

Type

The type of the color swatch:

*   **Advanced color**: use color names or images in PNG format.
    
*   **Metafields**: Use color codes or images in PNG format from metafields.
    

[Follow this instruction for more detailed](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-variant)

Width

Determines the width of the color swatch.

Height

Determines the height of the color swatch.

Corner radius

Set the radius of the color swatch's corners. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 1px (pixel).

[PreviousTerms and conditionschevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general/terms-and-conditions)
[NextVariant pickerchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general/variant-picker)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Customization option | Ella Documentation

**Customization options** are used to collect customization information for an item added to the cart. This information can be collected from the buyer on the product page and quick view.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Customization option**.
    

Setting

Description

Show in cart and checkout

Display the customization option in cart and checkout.

Type

Select which products the customization options to be shown. It can be for all products, products of a certain collection or products having listed tags.

Tags list

List out the tags to determine which products will be shown with customization options.

Collection

Choose a collection to show its products with customization options.

Text option's name

Fill in the name of the desired customization option for the text option.

File option's name

Fill in the name of the desired customization option for the file option.

circle-info

You need to go to the **Product Information** section and add the **Customization property** block to show the customization option on the product page and quick view.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FaaZmt558VghYcT0HPPwQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7058d2d-d778-4671-8853-8482460e195e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8234e49b&sv=2)

[PreviousVariant pickerchevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general/variant-picker)
[NextCustomer loginchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general/customer-login)

# Multiple Layouts | Ella Documentation

**Multiple layouts** allows you to create different structures and satisfies any specific styles for different kinds of business.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Multiple layouts.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FkI9S67lYYvodHrn08VH0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e302433-def4-4f95-bd82-e208c1bcf1f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12af61de&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvRMFcnTeTL65hJZCjuPN%252Fmulti-layouts.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2dcc0fc2-4ee1-4edf-9952-5ccdb580379c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5793ee6c&sv=2)

**Body**

Setting

Description

Layout

*   **Default**: Set the width of the body to its default size based on the viewport.
    
*   **Full width**: Set the width of the body to be full of the viewport.
    
*   **Boxed**: Set the width of the body to 1370px and and allow adding two banners to either side of the viewport.
    
*   **Custom width**: Manually set the width of the body in the range between 1200px and 1920px.
    

**Boxed layout**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FCHW0bWMRA5t9YVpeLdGQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6f36ad0-96ed-4a33-8d88-a02824636bd9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e5ba4e66&sv=2)

[Layout Boxed on Home 16arrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com//?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127365722)

These settings are only applicable when the '**Layout**' setting of the **Body** section is set to '**Boxed'**.

Setting

Description

Background color

The background color of an entire page.

Background image

The background image of an entire page.

Left banner

Upload image banner to the left of the entire page.

Left banner link

Specify the link for the left banner to redirect to.

Right banner

Upload image banner to the right of the entire page.

Right banner link

Specify the link for the right banner to redirect to.

**Menu mobile**

Setting

Description

Layout

*   **Default**: The mobile menu will share the same content as the menu setup on desktop.
    
*   **Custom**: The mobile menu will be customized to have icons and links that are different from those on desktop.
    

**Collection pages**

Setting

Description

Layout

*   **Default**: The Default Collection Layout comes with its filter facets on a sidebar. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/collections/new-in/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127365722)
    
*   **Express order**: The collection layout allows your customers to view and select their desired quantity of all the products on one page. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/collections/collection-home-1-2/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127365722)
    
*   **Full with**: The Full Width Collection Layout will have the filter facets lying on the top of the product showcase. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/collections/collection-home-01-3/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127365722)
    
*   **Masonry**: The collection layout allows the product items in the following row rise up to completely fill the gaps. It minimizes gaps between elements of varying height, creating a ‘Pinterest-like’ layout. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/collections/collection-home-01-5/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127365722)
    
*   **Right sidebar**: The layout of the collection page with the sidebar on the right side. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/collections/collection-home-01-4)
    
*   **Banner advertisement**: The collection page layout allows up to three additional image banners inside the product grid. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/collections/collection-home-01-6/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127365722)
    

**Collection list pages**

Setting

Description

Layout

*   **Default**: Collections will be displayed in a form of grid. The collection content displays below the collection image. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/collections?_ab=0&_fd=0&_sc=1&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **List:** Collections will be displayed line by line. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/collections?_ab=0&_fd=0&_sc=1&preview_theme_id=123378565171)
    
*   **Mansonry**: The collections list page layout allows the collection items in the following row rise up to completely fill the gaps. It minimizes gaps between elements of varying height, creating a ‘Pinterest-like’ layout. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/collections?_ab=0&_fd=0&_sc=1&preview_theme_id=123378630707)
    
*   **Grid**: Collections will be displayed in a form of grid with the collection name superimposed over the collection image. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/collections?_ab=0&_fd=0&_sc=1&preview_theme_id=123378663475)
    
*   **Full width**: Collections will be displayed 2 columns per row. The collection content displays on the right side of the collection image. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/collections?_ab=0&_fd=0&_sc=1&preview_theme_id=123378663475)
    

**Product pages**

Setting

Description

Layout

*   **Default**: The default layout of the product detail page. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/products/loremous-saliduar-a-cosmopolito/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **Full width**: The product page layout display product media as a scroll. To view all product images, simply scroll down. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/products/loremous-saliduar-a-cosmopolito-2/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127234650)
    
*   **Grid view**: The product page layout display product media as a grid. First row show two images and next row show one image. The same for the next rows. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/products/nulla-dinterdum-miverra-des-lacos-1/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127103578)
    
*   **Gallery**: The product page layout displays product media as a grid with four images and can be slid left to view the remaining product images. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/products/dinterdum-lorem-condimente/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123385806899)
    
*   **Left vertical thumbnails**: The product page layout shows product thumbnail slider to the left of the main product. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/products/naminos-dementus-a-dincidunto-4/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **Right vertical thumbs**: The product page layout shows product thumbnail slider to the right of the main product. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/products/dinterdum-pretium-condimento/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **Left/Right sidebar**: The product page layout shows the sidebar to the left/right of the main product. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/products/naminos-dementus-a-dincidunto-4/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **Horizontal tab without sidebar**: The product page layout displays product media as a grid with two images and can be slide left to view the remaining product images. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/products/dinterdum-lorem-condimente/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123385806899)
    

**Blog Pages**

Setting

Description

Layout

*   **Default**: Blogs are shown in group. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/blogs/blog-default/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **Simple**: Blogs are shown individually. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/blogs/blog/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **Full width**: The blogs will be displayed line by line. The blog post content is to the right side of the blog image on the first line and the second line is the opposite. The same for next lines. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/blogs/blog-full-width/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **Masonry**: The blog page layout allows the blog posts in the following row rise up to completely fill the gaps. It minimizes gaps between elements of varying height, creating a ‘Pinterest-like’ layout. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/blogs/blog-mansory/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    
*   **List**: The blogs will be displayed line by line with the content to the right side of the blog image. [Demoarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/blogs/blog-list/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)
    

**Password Layout**

Setting

Description

Layout

*   **Password 01**: The layout of the password page with the submit form on the left side and a background image on the right.
    
*   **Password 02**: The layout of the password page allows the submit form and the count down block to display superimposed over the background image.

# Customer login | Ella Documentation

This setting allow you can enable/disable the **Customer Login** sidebar.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FQRShUHHAb11YkVtIaYIt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D215ee7a8-4ade-44ee-86c0-7d89a7b6eaaf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b08f8b68&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Customer login**.
    

Setting

Description

Show customer login

Enable the Customer Login sidebar.

Login button

Select the style of the Login button:

*   Primary button
    
*   Secondary button
    
*   Tertiary button
    

Register Button

Select the style of the Register button:

*   Primary button
    
*   Secondary button
    
*   Tertiary button

# Pagination | Ella Documentation

Settings for page pagination such as blogs page.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Pagination**.
    

Setting

Description

Layout

Select the style for the pagination: **Style 1:** Pagination arrows are text "prev" and "next". **Style 2:** Pagination arrows are carets. **Style 3:** Pagination arrows are long-tailed.

Alignment

Align the Pagination cluster to the left, right or center of the products grid.

# Favicon | Ella Documentation

circle-info

You can use a free favicon generator website to create a custom favicon, or you can create your own. To find a favicon generator, search the internet for free favicon generator.

circle-info

The ideal size for a favicon is either 16x16 pixels or 32x32 pixels. If your favicon file is too large, then it will be reduced to 32x32 pixels when you upload it to Shopify

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General**.
    
4.  In the **Favicon image** area, click **Select image**.
    

Settings

Meaning

Favicon image

Upload an image to use as the favicon.

# Slider arrows | Ella Documentation

circle-info

Slideshow, Image Banner, Product Block, Product Recommendations and Recently Viewed Product Sections will have separate settings for navigation arrow positions.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Slider arrows**.
    

Setting

Description

Style

Select the style of the slider navigation arrows.

*   **Style 1:** Thin caret with large angle.
    
*   **Style 2:** Arrows have longer tails.
    
*   **Style 3:** Thick caret with small angle.
    
*   **Style 4**
    
*   **Style 5**
    
*   **Style 6**
    
*   **Style 7**
    
*   **Style 8**
    

Show arrow buttons when disabled

Show the arrows even when the slider has reached its end of items length.

Width

Determines the width of the slider navigation arrows.

Height

Determines the width of the slider navigation arrows.

Border width

Determine the thickness of the borders of the slider navigation arrows.

Corner radius

Set the radius of the slider navigation arrows' corners. Can be from 0% to 50%, increasing arithmetically of 1%.

Icon size

Determine the size of the arrow icon inside the border.

Horizontal position (unit % or px)

Positions of the slider navigation arrows horizontally relative to their slider.

# Slider dots | Ella Documentation

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Slider dots.**
    

Setting

Description

Style

Select the style of the slider navigation dots:

*   **Style 1:** Dots will simply styled with its background, border and hover state color.
    
*   **Style 2:** Dots group will also have a background layer.
    

Width

Determines the width of the slider navigation dots.

Height

Determines the height of the slider navigation dots.

Background opacity

Sets the opacity level for the background of the slider navigation dots.

_Note: For layout style 2_

# Install Theme 🎯 | Ella Documentation

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/install-theme#refer-our-video-for-full-instruction)

Refer our video for full instruction:

Instruction Video

> Below is a detailed instruction on how to install the Ella Shopify theme for your store. Halothemes also offers [**Professional Installation Services**](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/our-services/theme-installation-service)
>  for your store if you prefer assistance with the installation process.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/install-theme#preparing-theme-package)

P**reparing Theme Package**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

Remember: The package you download from Envato contains:

*   Ella Shopify 6.0
    
*   Child themes (will be removed when all child themes are added into Ella 6.0)
    
*   PSD file: We only provide PSD file of Ella default homepage
    

1.  Download the package from [themeforest.netarrow-up-right](https://1.envato.market/dokaB2)
     (the package is in zip format).
    
2.  Unzip the package you've just downloaded.
    
3.  Find this file: **ella-6.7.6-theme-source.zip** in the folder **Ella Shopify 6.0**, then you just need to upload **ella-6.7.6-theme-source.zip** file to your Shopify store.
    

If you want to **install child theme**, please go to the **corresponding theme folder of child theme.**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFPOBAaWwDmoD3AlYfRJr%252Fella%2520package.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f982e3f-4411-480c-9727-200373750097&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c170e76&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/install-theme#step-1-upload-theme-source)

Step 1: Upload Theme Source


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To install the theme:

1.  Please log in to your Shopify store, click **Online Store**.
    
2.  At **Theme Library**, click **Add theme**, choose **Upload zip file**.
    
3.  The **Upload Theme** dialog displays. Click **Add File or drop file to upload** to select the .zip file you want to upload.
    
4.  Click **Upload file**.
    
5.  Wait until the uploading process finishes. Then click **Publish** button to active the source to be live.
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/install-theme#step-2-upload-settings-data-for-home-page)

Step 2: Upload Settings Data For Home Page


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Home Page Layouts, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to download](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/install-theme#preset-for-home-page)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FeLSXAklt3WGdXCxkEZy1%252Fedit-code.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dede856e0-fb0b-41d9-af45-5c31077548ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cde30352&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to the "**Templates**" folder, open the "**index.json**" file, **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F8fdzg3KWdhMyPL958jxG%252Findex-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bea4fd9-df30-4fd0-ab80-251fcfdc4fb9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4546f4b2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/install-theme#step-3-upload-settings-data-for-theme-settings)

Step 3: Upload Settings Data For Theme Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up the same data for Theme Settings, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to download](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/installation/install-theme#preset-for-home-page)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FQDXSaEet1Srq13O6lnVR%252Fedit-code.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15f49d40-d70e-4581-bcb4-8fa5da945736&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b920f001&sv=2)

1.  Find folder **Config** **\->** Open file **settings\_data.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FHnya4w7sGOU6ugKtxmvr%252Fsettings-data-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D835213a3-bbee-4c8f-bc32-b33b1e1f893d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fef30394&sv=2)

# Recently Viewed Popup | Ella Documentation

**Recently viewed popup** also called as **Multitasking Function** which shows the products that customers have viewed recently, social media, and back to top.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Recently viewed popup.**
    

Settings

Meaning

Show recently viewed popup (Checkbox)

Toggle to show the Recently Viewed Popup.

Show recently viewed popup (Range slider)

Determine the timespan within which the products being seen are included in the Recently Viewed items list.

Content alignment on mobile

Select the item content alignment on the Recently Viewed Popup on the mobile device.

Maximum products to show

Maximum number of products displayed.

Show social media links

Toggle to show the social media links.

Font size

Set the font size for the social media title.

Show back to top button

Toggle to show the back to top button.

[PreviousPopupchevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/popup)
[NextBefore You Leavechevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/before-you-leave)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Notify Me When Out Of Stock | Ella Documentation

When a product is sold out, customers can submit their emails to receive an announcement when the product is available. Customer's emails are sent to the email you set up in Theme Setting. You will check your email and reply to customers manually.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F2HjD0f3xH6fJX7FmqJIc%252F20.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc93a36dd-bb4e-456f-a319-1444f71dfd07&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa5f31af&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Frc3d7C3gNvj2cksM5VBr%252F32.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6eb38cac-2430-458e-8b8c-8240df0b29d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7006135&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **'Notify me' when out of stock.**
    

Settings

Meaning

Show 'notify me' when out of stock

Toggle to show the popup to notify users when a particular item is available in stock. _Note: An email address identifies an email box to which messages are delivered._

Form Title

Fill in the title for the notification popup form.

Button style

There are 3 styles for the button in the notification popup form: **First button Second button Third button**

[PreviousBefore You Leavechevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/before-you-leave)
[NextAsk An Expertchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/ask-an-expert)

# Quick Search | Ella Documentation

**Quick Search** helps shoppers find the products, brands, collections, features, model numbers, and content that they care about.

circle-info

Ella's Quick Search is integrated with Predictive Search provided by Shopify, which allows buyers quickly search for desired products without any need to redirect to the Search Page. To learn about predictive search, refer to [Add predictive search to your themearrow-up-right](https://shopify.dev/themes/navigation-search/search/predictive-search)
.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fyw9EkUz8Pw12nNS0QrXs%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e476a6c-2bcc-40d5-bdf4-bf592cae813f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed79cefe&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Quick search.**
    

Setting

Description

Enable quick search feature

Enable Quick Search functionality on the theme.

Maximum products to show

Determine the maximum products to query for quick search.

Show on results page

Select the quick search to search for products only or also blog posts and pages.

[PreviousMulti-Level Categorieschevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/multi-level-categories)
[NextQuick Cart/ Quick Edit Cartchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/quick-cart-quick-edit-cart)

# Product badges | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FyENd0zkMoBf5wWc5KzQL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db616cd1e-863f-462f-bd39-e200e75be7a9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbc0d379&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> Product card -> Product badges**.
    

Setting

Description

Show product badges

Toggle the display of product badges (e.g., new, sale, bundle) on the product card.

Position

Select the desired position of the product badges either to the left or right side of the product card.

Vertical position

Determine the desired spacing of the badges from the card's top.

Horizontal position

Determine the desired spacing of the badges from the card's left/right side.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#new-badge)

New badge


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New badge** can be set up automatically by time right in editor or set up manually by tags in product admin.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5ljaeH2t2SAeNZdBZ1DU%252F15.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddda1fcea-a60a-4ebc-9101-86fa43fef6e2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2bb7c76a&sv=2)

Set up "New" label manually by tags

Setting

Description

Show new badge

Toggle to include 'new badge' in the product badges on product card.

New badge display mode

Select the method to apply 'new badge':

**Dynamic:** The algorithm will be applied to automatically decide the product is new or not. **Manual:** The products with tags including 'new' keyword will be shown with new badge.

New badge calculation period

Determine the time range in which the product is shown with new badge.

Maximum new badge to show

Determine the amount of products to have 'new badge'

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#sale-badge)

Sale badge


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Sale badge** shows up when the product is added both "**price**" and "**price at compare**".

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FR3EqCOuPPqgTRJPeOtoX%252FScreenshot_2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D251a6687-5661-47c9-a2d8-372c86bb03fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=679bbd9c&sv=2)

Setting

Description

Show sale badge

Toggle to include 'sale badge' in the product badges on product card.

Sale badge display mode

Select the display mode for the sale badge: **% discount Text Text + % discount**

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#show-sold-out-badge)

Show sold out badge


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Show sold out badge** shows up when the available quantity of the product is 0.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F0eYRHv2sqVAqGU49yBn6%252Fsold-out.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db724164c-6f28-4ddc-9e52-9690cb5eee6a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e18c537&sv=2)

Setting

Description

Show sold out badge

Toggle to include 'sold out badge' in the product badges on product card.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#custom-badge)

Custom badge


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom badge can display the label same for all products or different for each product. If a product has both a tag and a metafield set up, it will prioritize displaying the label according to the metafield.

Setting

Description

Show custom badge

Priorities when setting up metafields.

Toggle to include 'custom badge' in the product badges on product card.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#show-custom-badge-same-for-all-products)

\+ Show custom badge same for all products

**Custom badge** shows up when the product added a "**label**" tag.

The default name of this label is **custom label.** You can use this label with another name and [change text in **edit language**](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#how-to-change-the-name-of-badge-label-or-translate-it-in-another-language)
.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FdyW25hTLZhpZSsn4418d%252Fcustom-bag-c.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe4c1c65-4974-490e-b7c3-6914bce289a6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d11a3a1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#custom-badge-different-for-each-product)

**Custom badge** shows when the product added a "**custom badge**" metafield.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FScDULj6pXy734MRWZDcD%252Fcustom-bag-a.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54d47481-e8d4-4ca8-8f64-f5733b8f19b1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b8eab69&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#create-a-metafield-for-custom-badge)

Create a metafield for custom badge

1.  From your shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FqnaCnG5vQ9nBpztcyRbF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc03464ba-8c91-4232-9641-9a97edfcc1b8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2de6726&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FMu2MMAbnePIwzk5lpDJj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a1bddfe-6efe-4aac-8067-ef35e6e48514&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2fb8c97a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/product-badges#how-to-insert-content-for-custom-badge-metafield)

How to insert content for custom badge metafield?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the text that you want for "**Custom badge**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOjH3aVJyFZH3nuDENQbv%252Fcustom-bag-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60f8cb03-5f28-4410-af6b-6f3e02a22c5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65961082&sv=2)

# Multi-Level Categories | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FVJU0k51oFLPSjqgZy0c9%252F20.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df53eea88-fc2b-4600-a022-48588f508d43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f92e80c&sv=2)

Ella offers Multi Level Category Filter/ Year Make Model module for free. To edit and setup this module on your site, please follow our instruction below:

Go to **Navigation** to create a YMM menu you will use for this module. You only can use 3 levels of filter options corresponding with 3 levels of menu.

# Someone Purchased Notification Popup | Ella Documentation

**Someone purchased notification popup** lets visitors see your products more frequently and have a belief that their favorite items were purchased by other customers.

circle-exclamation

This function cannot get real data from your purchase. It is using fake data, if you don't want to use, you can delete it.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F8HOFeVqZVAWr38luO1vt%252F25.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db342aedf-9396-4088-826a-7d2a887f9212&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28c355d1&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Someone purchased notification popup.**
    

Settings

Meaning

Show someone purchased notification popup

Toggle the feature to show the popup telling someone has purchased a particular item.

Show someone purchased notification popup on mobile

Toggle the feature to show the popup telling someone has purchased a particular item on mobile device.

Desktop content position

Select the position on the right or left side of the viewport. The settings is for Desktop device only.

Change slide every

Determine the time between each slide transition.

Products list

Select a set products for the function to randomize each time the popup shows up.

Locations

Enter the list of locations for the function to randomize each time the popup shows up. Each list item must be separated with a |. _Example: blackburn, UK | melbourne, AU | sydney, AU_

Times

Enter the list of times for the function to randomize each time the popup shows up. Each list item must be separated with a |. _Example: 20 minutes | 50 minutes | 2 hours_

# Before You Leave | Ella Documentation

**Before you leave** will show up after your customers don’t have any actions like clicking or hovering on the store. The store owner can set up the time when it would show in Theme Setting. This feature can show the promotion content, upsell products, discount campaign to attract visitor’s attention in case they want to leave.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F1eZpKpjU7TfLjWOFmWc7%252FBEFORE-YOU-LEAVE.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e004164-5dee-416b-84ec-af5345c98a48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0f3be0d&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Before you leave.**
    

Settings

Meaning

Show before you leave

Toggle to show the Before You Leave popup to remind users.

Position

Select the position of the popup to appear to the right or left of the viewport.

Show after (minutes)

Determine the timespan to show the popup since the stop of user's interaction or tab navigation.

Logo

Select the brand logo to appear on the popup.

Background image

Select an image for the top part background of the popup.

Content

Enter the content for the popup. HTML can be inserted to create more complicated layout for the popup content.

Collection

Select a collection to show as Recommended Products on the popup.

Maximum products to show

Determine the maximum number of products within the collection to show on the popup.

Show back to store button

Toggle the button allowing users to navigate back to a store page on clicked.

Style

There are 3 styles for the continue shopping button: **First button Second button Third button**

Link

Specify the link for the Back To Store button to navigate to.

# Ask An Expert | Ella Documentation

**Ask an expert** enables customers to PRIVATELY connect with EXPERTS (Store owner) to get direct advice or insights on any questions. When customers submit the form, the information will be sent to the email you set up in Setting. You will check your email and reply to customers manually.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FnRwBMa1HQCIDG60W3zSH%252F21.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1318fcc-2dff-4277-9f17-50242520b974&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=422b21a7&sv=2)

# Custom JS | Ella Documentation

JS (Javascript) is a scripting or programming language that allows you to implement complex features on web pages.

We attached a JS file in Ella source so that you can customize the site by yourself.

**Step 1: Enable the Custom JS file:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme Settings ->** scroll down to the bottom -> **Custom JS.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F6zP064dvTtZFu15brKlk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2304c1b2-6ca2-4731-9329-6b0f0f803e87&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=972f84f9&sv=2)

**Step 2: Edit the Custom JS file:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
2.  Find folder **Assets->** Open file **custom.js**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FXHaFETvTZuWcVzL4uPCq%252F8.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D256caa8d-b768-46fb-9433-3105b0e1e3da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2a026e4&sv=2)

# How to set up a different language? | Ella Documentation

circle-info

Language function is a default function in Shopify themes, not a custom built-in function.

By default, we copy the English texts for other languages to avoid any issues with 'translate missing' when switching to another language from English.

Please follow the instructions below to fill in the texts in your preferred language. While this process requires manual setup, it is easy to do.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-a-different-language#change-the-default-language-of-your-online-store)

Change the default language of your online store

You can change the default language of your store. Your default store language is used in your Shopify admin and in your store's checkout and theme.

**Steps:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** > **Languages**.
    
2.  In **Published languages**, click **Change default** beside the language that is your current default language.
    
3.  Select a language from the menu.
    
4.  Click **Save**.
    

**Note**

If you publish a language to your store without adding translations, then you'll receive a message prompting you to add translations. Languages that are published without adding additional translations will only show the provided translations for the theme and checkout, and the default language for all other content.

**Steps:**

From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes** -> **Edit default theme content**

Start translate the English texts within the red highlight tabs into your language or you can click Localize button to translate by the app:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FBJpbtTRxe4AIbFjVjLYk%252FScreenshot_11.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e146e6b-2321-4ee0-8e11-4706c5d123bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2f4cedd0&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FEd8Bxar6913Hhprd0b9M%252FScreenshot_13.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0cbec5ca-0f3d-4d10-b183-0b26de21479d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0b69c9b&sv=2)

**At here, you will replace the English texts by your preferred language and Save your changes.**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FGVMEzAUfjCULK5REFMXf%252Fella-languages.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D587543a9-e8d3-4db2-ba04-5c518c0b8af6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a075395d&sv=2)

[PreviousTheme Languagechevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language)
[NextHow to set up Multiple Languages?chevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Brand image | Ella Documentation

Upload Brand Image on Product Cards: Showcase brand logos to build trust and boost recognition.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Ffd7a0easBGc1COE3QeAM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2606c551-5c87-46f5-895e-276860154162&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20aa028d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/brand-image#how-do-i-set-up-a-brand-image-on-the-product-card)

How do I set up a brand image on the product card?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Upload image with the same name as the vendor-\[vendor-name\].\[img format\].

**Vendor-name** convention: lower cap and use "**\-**" to replace white space.

**Img format** convention: use one of the following formats — **JPG**, **PNG**, or **WebP**.

**For example**: with the vendor Metaly, the image name you can set is **vendor-metaly.jpg** or **vendor-metaly.png**, or **vendor-metaly.webp**.

[PreviousMarqueechevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/marquee)
[NextTheme Languagechevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Free Shipping Calculator Message | Ella Documentation

**Free shipping calculator message** shows progressive bar with message when customers put more items in their shopping carts.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F1xjjYI1U67OyGsywTMrJ%252F23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7eb9255a-86ff-4c95-af52-af086f53ed13&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8dbd1cf6&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Free shipping calculator message.**
    

Show free shipping calculator message

Toggle the alert for the free shipping message and calculation bar.

Type

There are 2 types for free shipping calculator message functionality:

**Discount**

**Shipping and delivery**

Enter total order price to offer free shipping

Enter the threshold of the total order amount to achieve free shipping.

_Note: the currency is automatically the shop currency._

Height

Determine the height of the free shipping calculation bar ranging from 10 to 20px.

Rounded border

Determine the roundness of the border of the bar ranging from 0 to 100px.

Show percent

Show the percent of the calculation bar.

Show shipping truck icon

Toggle to show the truck icon running along with the calculation bar.

Text color

Apply color for the bar percent text.

Background color

Apply default color for the bar background.

Background color < 30%

Apply color for the bar background when the percent is less than 30%.

Background color < 60%

Apply color for the bar background when the percent is larger than 30% but less than 60%.

Background color < 100%

Apply color for the bar background when the percent is larger than 60% but less than 100%.

Background color = 100%

Apply color for the bar background when the bar reaches 100%.

[PreviousCountdownchevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown)
[NextSomeone Purchased Notification Popupchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/someone-purchased-notification-popup)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Quick Shop | Ella Documentation

**Quick Shop** function helps customers add the product to the cart quickly. They can purchase the item immediately on the home page or collection page without visiting the product page.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> Product card -> Quick shop**.
    

Setting

Description

Enable quick shop

Enable/Disable the quick shop functionality on product card.

Type

Choose option for the Quick Shop layout:

**Option 1**

**Option 2**

**Option 3**

**Bulk**

_Note: Bulk is optimized for items purchased in higher quantities._

*   **Option 1** will show as this below design: Automatically activate variant image on product card if available

*   **Option 2** will show as this below design:
    

circle-info

# Adding custom CSS to your theme | Ella Documentation

CSS (Cascading Style Sheets) is coded file that selects elements of your page and controls their presentation. Think of your custom template's HTML as the bones of your website and the CSS as the skin of your site.

Please refer this article from Shopify for Adding custom CSS to your theme: [https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/online-store/themes/theme-structure/extend/add-cssarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/online-store/themes/theme-structure/extend/add-css)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/adding-custom-css-to-your-theme#add-custom-css-in-theme-settings)

Add Custom Css in Theme Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom CSS can be added to your entire theme that affects all pages in your online store except the **Checkout** page. For example, you can change the way that buttons are displayed across your entire store.

**Steps:**

1.  In your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** > **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> CUSTOM CSS**.
    
4.  Add your code and click **Save**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FccGTu5m6rRX6jLirPBAf%252Fcustom-css.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7638af44-29eb-4b7b-af59-fde8e5c784d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=555bea7a&sv=2)

circle-info

Your css will be saved in **settings\_data.json** file

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRmaZWhGQIgnaDShVqqRU%252Fcustom-css-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3adf465-b901-44a4-aa55-3f14f399a75e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=694627e4&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/adding-custom-css-to-your-theme#add-custom-css-in-section)

Add Custom Css in Section


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom CSS can also be added to a specific section of your theme. For example, you can apply a custom font size or a background color to a single section.

**Steps:**

1.  In your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** > **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click the section that you want to add CSS to.
    
4.  At the bottom of the section properties panel, click **Custom CSS**.
    
5.  Add your code and click **Save**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Ff4U01jOEIdxTbG6bNweo%252Fcustom-css-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1bf1158c-d158-454d-b1df-42614ee9bb1e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e856c8ce&sv=2)

circle-info

Your css will be saved in **index.json** file

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Ftkk0Yu8FMSCckoEItCX7%252Fcustom-css-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd02f6f01-17de-4f2a-aeed-42d51df979b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1da767c&sv=2)

[PreviousAnimationschevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/animations)
[NextCustom JSchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/custom-js)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Add Custom Css in Theme Settings](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/adding-custom-css-to-your-theme#add-custom-css-in-theme-settings)
    
*   [Add Custom Css in Section](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/adding-custom-css-to-your-theme#add-custom-css-in-section)

# Multiple Currencies | Ella Documentation

circle-info

We have 3 options for currencies: **Shopify payments**, **Multiple currencies** and **Auto currencies**.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/multiple-currencies#how-to-edit-the-html-for-currency-formatting)

How to edit the HTML for Currency formatting?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Settings**.
    
2.  Scroll down to **Store currency** area, you'll see your **Currency** settings.
    
3.  Click **Change formatting** to open the **Currency Formatting** section.
    
4.  Find **HTML with currency** and **HTML without currency** formats in the section.
    

HTML for Currency Formatting

Copy

    <span class=money>${{amount}}</span>

Email for Currency Formatting

Copy

    ${{amount}}

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FYaplJAWul0zE3hcD84j2%252FScreenshot_18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8ee1ec8-6b0c-4caf-b676-d485ca3ad6e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2debf197&sv=2)

circle-info

**Remember**: We set up USD as the default currency. If you use another currency, please replace it with the corresponding one. In addition, please enter correct currency formatting, otherwise it'll cause issues related to other functions like "**Add To Cart Function"**, for example.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/multiple-currencies#set-up-currencies)

Set Up Currencies


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ella Theme supports **Shopify multiple currencies** as well as theme built-in currency features. Please follow our instructions below to set up currencies for your site:

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/multiple-currencies#shopify-payments)

S**hopify payments**

This feature is only available for stores using **Shopify payments**. Please follow instruction of Shopify to enable Shopify Payments. For more information, see [How to enable Shopify Paymentsarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/payments/shopify-payments/multi-currency/setup)
.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Multiple currencies.**
    
4.  Turn on "**Shopify payments**".
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/multiple-currencies#multiple-currencies)

**Multiple currencies**

This feature is a built-in feature of Ella Theme which allows you to show multiple currencies on your site**.**

circle-info

This option will not have automatic currency feature by location

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\-> Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Multiple currencies.**
    
4.  Turn on "**Multiple currencies**".
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/multiple-currencies#auto-currencies)

A**uto currencies**

This feature is a built-in feature of Ella Theme which allows your customers to see the item price on their own currency. When you enable this feature, currency selector on your site will be disabled, customers will see price in their currency by location.

circle-info

At checkout page, currency will be the default currency of your store

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Multiple currencies.**
    
4.  Turn on "**Auto currencies**".
    

Description

Enable currencies

Enable/Disable the currencies function.

Enable currency format

Cart and checkout prices always show currency codes. Example: $1.00 USD.

Select a currency function

Select a currency function: **Shopify payment Multiple currencies Auto currencies** _Note: Only available for stores with shopify payments. Link_ [_here_arrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/payments/shopify-payments/multi-currency/setup)
_._

Currency code

Add your currency codes _Note: Separate your currency codes with a space. Use the ISO 4217 3-letter currency code. Click_ [_here_arrow-up-right](http://www.xe.com/iso4217.php)
 _for a complete list of currency codes. Example: CAD USD._

_For this functionality to work in your shop, you need to edit your money formats according to_ [_these instructions_arrow-up-right](http://help.shopify.com/en/themes/customization/currencies)
_. (Please specify where the money format is located.)_

SVG icon for currency code

Add SVG code

[PreviousHow to set up Multiple Languages?chevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages)
[NextMulti-Level Categorieschevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/multi-level-categories)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Saved price | Ella Documentation

The s**aved price** is the amount of money saved between the original price and the sale price.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Saved price.**
    

Setting

Description

Show saved price

Show saved price feature on your website.

# Dynamic browser tab title | Ella Documentation

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Dynamic browser tab title**.
    

Setting

# Marquee | Ella Documentation

If the Type **"Text"** option is selected, the Product Marquee runs if the field is not empty. Whereas **"Sale Text"** or **"Sale Discount"** is selected, the function only runs if the product is on sale.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fdl2ezBI7AqUahdrrpIyP%252Fproduct-marquee.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5881a2cb-28bb-4459-acea-d1a1c1e55e2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd987f1b&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> Product card -> Marquee**.
    

Description

Show marquee

Enable/Disable the marquee functionality on the product card.

Background

Set the background color of the marquee.

Color

Set the text color of the marquee.

Type

Choose option for Marquee data: **Text Sale text Sale discount Metafield** _Note: 'Text' will be applied to all products. 'Sale text' and 'sale discount' will only be applied to products on sale._

Text

Set text for marquee with Text option

Font size

Set the font size of the marquee.

Font size on mobile

Set the font size on mobile of the marquee.

Font weight

Set the font weight of the marquee.

Text style

Set the text style of the marquee.

Font style

Set the font style of the marquee.

You can use **Metafields** to show scrolling text by each product.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/marquee#how-to-add-new-metafields)

**How to add new Metafields?**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom Data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    
3.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fi6IycmOxS53HWvcfKfG8%252Fproduct-marquee-metafield.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69581d9e-033a-4345-8b5e-b31261b4ca14&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=836ef0a4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/marquee#how-to-insert-content-for-product-metafields)

How to insert content for Product Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the text that for "**Product Card Marquee**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fdex9pP2qcSdQOTNHLOow%252Fproduct-marquee-metafield-product.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ce85503-a636-4cd7-9491-58af1b0ffe48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f704a80&sv=2)

circle-info

You can use [Bulk Editorarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/shopify-admin/productivity-tools/bulk-editing)
 to edit multiple products.

[NextBrand imagechevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/brand-image)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Header For Mobile / Tablet | Ella Documentation
