# Countdown | Ella Documentation

**Countdown** shows customers the period of time when the product is on the promotion.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FClQ0PmfXbs0Im1FhCwAy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df03891d1-2900-47b1-b47f-825305de9fd5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29a75b35&sv=2)

circle-info

Ella offers 3 ways to show countdown:

*   For All Products.
    
*   For Each Product.
    
*   For Collection.
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#for-all-products)

For All Products


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Countdown.**
    
4.  Choose **Type** as **For all products.**
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#for-each-product)

For Each Product


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Countdown.**
    
4.  Choose **Type** as **For each product.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#how-to-add-a-new-metafields)

H**ow to add a new Metafields?**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** **\->** **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FBuFwpBv2o3fPUJiC4H0F%252Fmeta-field.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58a9be46-483a-461d-ba87-7bef16a76dce&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24646a94&sv=2)

1.  Please enter the correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FrBfQ0Uq9fcVEIFA3hPac%252Fcountdown-1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De83eab94-9a8d-4ff9-b09f-f00b9043af0b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=752649ee&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#how-to-insert-content-for-product-metafields)

How to insert content for Product Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields,** you need to insert timer structure for "**Countdown**".
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FB8NMZfdQEjPIKwaXqtB5%252F23.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f5841c3-094e-448e-81d8-8c3548bf2ca4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e06afd23&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#for-collection)

For Collection


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Countdown.**
    
4.  Choose **Type** as **For the collection.**
    
5.  Select **Collection**.
    

Settings

Meaning

Show countdown

Enable the countdown functionality on your website.

Type

There are 5 types to define which product is displayed countdown: **For all Products For each product For the collection**

Text

Fill in the text you want to use for the countdown.

End date

Fill in the date and time the countdown will end. _Example: Dec 31, 2024 18:00:00 Note: - Oct (mm): This is abbreviation of October and please use the abbreviation of months in this countdown structure. - Please use 1 white space among mm dd yyyy._

Collection

Select a collection that you want all products in this collection to display the countdown (only for the collection type).

Style

There are 3 styles for countdown layout: **Style 1 Style 2 Style 3**

[PreviousQuick Viewchevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/quick-view)
[NextFree Shipping Calculator Messagechevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/free-shipping-calculator-message)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [For Each Product](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#for-each-product)
    
*   [How to add a new Metafields?](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#how-to-add-a-new-metafields)

*   [For Collection](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/countdown#for-collection)
    

Copy

    Name: Countdown
    Namespace and key: c_f.countdown
    Select content type: Text

# Popup | Ella Documentation

Once customers visit the site, they can sign up a **Newsletter popup** to receive a discount/promotion or information of New Arrivals.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FlHFoGzDrExpK3eCoZ0o3%252F28.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1562cf28-0206-4f76-89bd-63814864d8ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f933f3a&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/popup#how-to-work)

How to work


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a customer submits their information through the Newsletter popup, their details are automatically saved in the **Customers** section of your Shopify Admin. This allows you to collect and manage the email addresses of interested customers in one place.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FhiegyMFSIT0U2Skd3vGj%252Fnewsletter-customer.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb841269-ac51-4875-851d-96baa1f119b3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3bc1fd83&sv=2)

However, Shopify does not automatically send emails to your customers. When you have a promotion or updates to share, you will need to manually send emails to your customers. You can do this by exporting the list of customer emails and using email marketing tools to create and send your campaigns.

This approach gives you full control over your email communications, ensuring that only relevant and timely updates reach your audience.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/popup#how-to-set-up)

How to set up


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** P**opup.**
    

Settings

Meaning

Show popup

Toggle to show the Popup.

Style popup

Select a style for the popup:

**Newsletter**

**Promotion**

Show again after

Determine the time span between each automatical showing of the popup.

Delay time

Determine the delay time for the popup to automatically shows up.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/popup#newsletter)

Newsletter

Settings

Meaning

Show image

Toggle to show image on the popup.

Image

Select an image for the popup.

Link

Specify the link for the image to redirects to on clicked.

Title

Enter the title for the popup form.

Description

Enter the description for the popup description.

Note

Enter the text for the decline.

**Button**

Type

Select the behavior of the popup form button. The options are:

**Default (subscription is managed by Shopify server)**

**Custom link (to any URL that merchants specify).**

Link

Specify the link for the **Custom link** to redirect to. _Note: Use for custom link._

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/popup#promotion)

Promotion

Settings

Meaning

Image

Select an image for the popup.

Link

Specify the link for the image to redirects to on clicked.

Title

Set the title for your banner promotion

Discount label

Set the discount label for your banner promotion

Additional discount info

Set the additional discount info for your banner promotion

Discount code text

Set the discount code text for your banner promotion

Discount code description

Set the discount code description for your banner promotion

Note

Set the note for your banner promotion

Button label

Set the button label for your banner promotion

Link

Specify the link for the **Custom link** to redirect to. _Note: Use for custom link._

Show social media links

Displays the social media links

**Recommended products**

Show recommended products

Displays the recommended products

Title

Set the title for your recommended products

Products list

Choose products to feature in the recommendations

Button label

Set the button label for your recommended products

Link

Specify the link for the **Custom link** to redirect to. _Note: Use for custom link._

# Trusted image | Ella Documentation

**Trust Image** shows custom images on Product Page, Quick View and Cart Page.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> General -> Trusted image.**
    

Setting

Description

**Product page/Quick view**: Image 1

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 1 on product page/quick view.

**Product page/Quick view**: Image 2

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 2 on product page/quick view.

**Product page/Quick view**: Image 3

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 3 on product page/quick view.

**Product page/Quick view**: Image 4

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 4 on product page/quick view.

**Cart page**: Image 1

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 1 on cart page.

**Cart page**: Image 2

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 2 on cart page.

**Cart page**: Image 3

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 3 on cart page.

**Cart page**: Image 4

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 4 on cart page.

**Cart page**: Image 5

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 5 on cart page.

**Cart page**: Image 6

Upload an image to use as the trusted image 6 on cart page.

# Set up for product card | Ella Documentation

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings -> Product card**
    

Description

Image ratio

Select the image ratio type for the product card:

**Adapt to image:** the image size on product card will scale according to the image actual size. **Portrait:** The image of the product card will have a height more than its width. The ratio of the width and height can be adjusted with the "Image height (%)" setting below. **Square:** The image of the product card will be a square.

Portrait aspect ratio

Fill in the desired ratio of the height of the product card media in %. _Note: Use for portrait ratio._

Image fit

Select the image fit type for the product card:

**Original:** The image will keep its current scale ratio to adapt. **Fit conten**t**:** The image will scale to cover up the full area of set product card image with retained ratio. **Fill:** The image will scale to scale up until the width or height reached the width or height of the set product card image with retained ratio.

Enable image swap

Toggle the functionality when the product card image is hovered, it will swap to the second image.

Play video on hover

Only works with MP4 video.

The same as Product Image Swap but for video if there is any mp4 video attached to the product.

Enable product image loading effect

Toggle the display of placeholder when the image is being loaded due to lazy load.

Show vendor

Toggle to show or hide product vendor.

Show price

Toggle to show or hide product price.

Show price percentage

Toggle to show or hide the percentage by which the product price has been discounted.

Show size variants

Toggle to show or hide product size variant.

Size variant style

Select the style for the product card size variant:

**Style 01 Style 02**

Show text 'more sizes available'

Toggle to show or hide text "more sizes available".

'More sizes available' text size

Determine the font size for the text 'more sizes available'.

Show the color name in the product name

Toggle to show or hide the color variant name after the product name.

Color name style

Select the style for the color variant name after the product name on the product card: **Style 01 Style 02**

Color name size

Determine the font size for the color variant name after the product name on the product card. _Note: Only for color name style 2._

Show compare

Toggle the display of compare checkbox on product card.

Hide compare on home page

Toggle the display of compare checkbox on product card for homepage.

Compare style

Select the display type of product compare on product card:

**Default Icon**

Show wishlist

Toggle to show or hide product wishlist on tablet and desktop.

Show wishlist on mobile

Toggle to show or hide product wishlist on mobile.

Show background for icon

Toggle to show or hide background for wishlist icon.

Show quick view

Toggle to show or hide product quick view on tablet and desktop.

Show quick view on mobile

Toggle to show or hide product quick view on mobile.

Quick view style

Select the display type of quick view button on product card:

**Default:** The quick view button is shown in the center of the product card when hovered. **Icon:** The quick view eye icon button is grouped with the wishlist button to the right of left side.

Quick view & wishlist position

Select the desired position of the quick view and wishlist buttons cluster either on the right or left side of product card.

Content alignment

Select the desired position of content on the right or left side or center of product card.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/set-up-for-product-card#product-image-swap)

Product image swap


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Product image swap** is a feature which allows adding a product image hover effect. In other words, it flips or changes a product image on hover.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPfcstBeTVALjBndF66Qz%252F12.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3840510e-11ab-437f-886f-2bcdc2318eda&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59961cb&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/set-up-for-product-card#product-video-swap)

Product video swap


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Product video swap** is a feature which allows adding a product video hover effect. In other words, it plays a product image on hover.

circle-info

This feature works with products having MP4 video only.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F0EvZFnzic2PgYFXPvTgS%252F13.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0a0d345-5e87-4f4d-9982-b1072070e83a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b1cacff&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-card/set-up-for-product-card#product-image-loading-effect)

Product image loading effect


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWh29hedaN6ePm9YGJJVt%252F14.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d4b31bb-3338-468d-a291-096342e1d7ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8001354&sv=2)

# Label For Menu | Ella Documentation

circle-info

Ella offers 3 labels for menu: New, Hot and Sale. You can setup label for menu level 1, menu level 2 or menu level 3.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FzNRU9LnXm6znruVkIR2F%252F111.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59643c9d-5bbc-4a8b-92a8-a0b2e05e5ed4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab229bbe&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  In the **Header** **Nav** section -> click **Menu** block to see the settings of Menu open, scroll to **Label On Menu**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOA55uZgvhFbkL0YeP776%252Fmenu-label.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5150d209-e729-4647-8c70-2d7d264489d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=831ecfc0&sv=2)

circle-info

Use "," to separate Menu items if you have multiple items.

For example: Demo, Brand.

# How to set up Multiple Languages? | Ella Documentation

Before setting up Multiple Languages, please refer to these links for reference:

*   [Localization and translationarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/markets/languages#changing-the-default-language-of-your-online-store)
    
*   [Managing languagesarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/markets/languages/manage-languages)
    
*   [Shopify Translate & Adapt apparrow-up-right](https://shopify.pxf.io/3P6XkB)
    

circle-info

Language function is a default function in Shopify themes, not a custom built-in function.

To use Multi Language Function, you must install an App. Shopify releases [Translate & Adapt apparrow-up-right](https://shopify.pxf.io/3P6XkB)
 to support you translate 2 languages automatically for free. Here are the key features:

*   Manually add, edit, and review translations with the side-by-side editor.
    
*   **Auto-translate 2 languages** with Google Translate (cloud.google.com/translate).
    
*   Adapt content to reflect spelling and messaging variations between markets.
    
*   Localize directly from the theme editor, or any resource page in your admin.
    
*   Manage localized store content seamlessly from your Shopify admin.
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#how-to-set-up-multiple-languages)

How to set up Multiple Languages?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow our instruction video

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Multiple languages.**
    
4.  Click "**Enable Right To Left Layout**" to show Right To Left layout if your language requires RTL
    

Description

Enable right to left layout

Enable/Disable Right To Left layout

ISO codes list for RTL languages

Add the ISO code of the language you want to use RTL layout. _Note: Separate each language ISO code with a ','. Eg: ar, ha, he._

_List out language ISO codes to automatically switch to RTL layout: ar:(Arabic); dv:(Dhivehi,Maldivian); ha:(Hausa); he:(Hebrew); ku:(Kurdish/Sorani); fa:(Persian/Farsi); ur:(Urdu); ps:(Pashto); yi:(Yiddish)_

Enable multiple languages

Enable/Disable multiple languages function _Note: When configuring a language in the customization settings, it's important to also establish the same language preference within the administrative settings._

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#ready-to-translate)

Ensure that you're ready to translate

You must provide the translations when adding languages to your store. Before you add a new language, ensure that you have your translations ready, or that you have a translation app installed and have assigned the language to a market.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#add-new-language)

Add new languages to your online store

Before you begin, make sure your store meets the [requirements for selling in multiple languagesarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/markets/languages#requirements)
.

**Steps:**

**Note**

If you need to create a new active market, then follow the steps to [add a marketarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/markets/managing-markets#add-a-market)
.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** > **Languages**.
    
2.  Click **Add Language**.
    
3.  Choose a language from the drop-down menu, then click **Add**.
    
4.  Select an active market to add your language to.
    
5.  Do either of the following:
    
    *   Use the [Translate & Adapt apparrow-up-right](https://apps.shopify.com/translate-and-adapt)
         to [import your translated contentarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/markets/languages/translate)
         into Shopify.
        
    *   Visit the [Shopify App Storearrow-up-right](https://apps.shopify.com/collections/works-with-shopify-markets?app_integration_pos=off&app_integration_shopify_checkout=off&category=store-design-internationalization&pricing=all&requirements=off&sort_by=collection_position)
         and install a translation app to your store. Follow the steps in the app to translate your online store's content and publish new languages.
        
    
6.  Click **Preview** to view different languages in your online store. You can preview both published and unpublished languages.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwTN2NFWkGtb611M43l5z%252F17.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e24664c-2a23-4565-a8fa-16f2c55da13e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77dc4cdc&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fh1Zq0nXepYTNTt4S2zW3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd288ea39-ea1b-4892-bb45-07958f9798c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87adce44&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FjJJaeoTr513Hl7JcyHuq%252FTranslation.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf96d52f-564a-4586-8a3e-f6375fada59d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a872523&sv=2)

**Note**

Adding a language only adds translations in [supported languagesarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/markets/languages/translate#available-translations)
 to supported themes and checkouts. If you want to add translations to other store content, then you need to import translations or use an app.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#publish-a-language-to-your-online-store)

Publish a language to your online store

**Steps:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** > **Languages**.
    
2.  In **Unpublished languages**, click **Publish** beside the language that you want to make available to customers in your store.
    
3.  Click **Save**.
    

**Note**

If you publish a language to your store without adding translations, then you'll receive a message prompting you to add translations. Languages that are published without adding additional translations will only show the provided translations for the theme and checkout, and the default language for all other content.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#manage-markets-languages)

Manage languages for markets

By default, each new market that you create uses your store's default language.

You need to assign newly published languages to a market before they become visible to visitors on your online store.

**Add a language to a market**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** > **Languages**.
    
2.  Click **More actions** beside the language that you want to add to a market.
    
3.  Click **Add to market**.
    
4.  Click **Done**.
    

**Remove a language from a market**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** > **Languages**.
    
2.  Click **More actions** beside the language that you want to remove from a market.
    
3.  Click **Remove**.
    
4.  Click **Done**.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#unpublish-a-language-in-your-online-store)

Unpublish a language in your online store

You can also unpublish a language, which hides the language from customers. Any links to the store in that particular language result in a 404 “Page not found” error, so [create redirectsarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/online-store/menus-and-links/url-redirect#import-your-url-redirects)
 for any of your unpublished languages.

**Steps:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** > **Languages**.
    
2.  In **Published languages**, click **Unpublish** beside the language that you want to make unavailable.
    
3.  Click **Unpublish**.
    

By unpublishing a language, you also remove that language from any markets that it was added to.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#delete-a-language-in-your-online-store)

Delete a language in your online store

If you're confident that you don't need translations in that language, then you can also delete the language. Deleting a language also deletes all translations of that language permanently. If a language is re-enabled in the future, then the translations need to be added again.

**Steps:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** > **Languages**.
    
2.  In **Unpublished languages**, click the delete icon beside the unpublished language that you want to remove from your store.
    
3.  Click **Delete**.
    

By deleting a language, you also remove that language from any markets that it was added to.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/theme-language/how-to-set-up-multiple-languages#change-the-default-language-of-your-online-store)

# Quick View | Ella Documentation

**Quick View** allows your customers to see more details about a product and add it to their cart without having to go to the individual product page, leading to a more fluid checkout flow.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FLLyV96YqPxymYJQeD3J2%252F19.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D523a3813-d3fc-4f3c-b37f-c98ca92a408d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a2cf788e&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Quick view.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/quick-view#thumbnails)

**Thumbnails**

Settings

Meaning

Layout

Select the layout for the quick view popup content. **Show thumbnails on the left Show thumbnails on the right Show thumbnails on the bottom Hide thumbnails**

Maximum thumbnails to show

Determine the number of thumbnail to visible at a time in the thumbnail slider.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/quick-view#image)

Image

Settings

Meaning

Image ratio

Select the ratio type of the product image. **Adapt to image Portrait Square**

Portrait aspect ratio

Determine the ratio of the width / height of the image if the Portrait option of Product Image Ratio is selected.

Show zoomed image

Toggle the image zooming when hovered.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/quick-view#badge)

Meaning

Set the text color of the title.

Show zoomed image

Enable the zoom functionaly of the main image.

###

Fill in the product quantity list that will appear in the Sold in last period function.

Hours

Fill in the 'hours' list that will appear in the Sold in last period function.

Text color

Set the text color of the Sold in last period function.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/quick-view#short-description)

Short description

Settings

Meaning

Show short description

Enable the short description in the quick view.

Short description word count

Set maximum number of words for the short description.

Font size

Set the font size of the short description.

Text color

Set the text color of the short description.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/quick-view#price)

Price

Settings

Set the font size of the price.

Enable the SKU in the quick view.

Enable the barcode in the quick view.

Enable the availability in the quick view.

Enable the type in the quick view.

Enable the stock levels functionality in the quick view.

There are 5 options for the size chart: Product type Product vendor Metafield Custom image Custom page

Image type

# Product Colors | Ella Documentation

Here you can change color for: **Product card, Size option, Swatch option, Hot stock, Wishlist, Compare, Quick View, Action button, Badges**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Product colors.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-colors#set-up-for-product-card)

Set up for Product card

Settings

Meaning

Vendor

Sets the color of the product vendor on the product card.

Title

Sets the color of the product title on the product card.

Title Color

Sets the color of the product title on the product card for hover state.

Price

Sets the color of the product price on the product card.

Sale price

Sets the color of the product sale price on the product card.

Compare price

Sets the color of the product compare price on the product card.

Countdown text

Sets the text color of the countdown block on the product card.

Countdown background

Sets the bacground color of the countdown block on the product card.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/product-colors#size-option)

Size option

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FiReSwaOcCcDFDBhv3973%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb0aefb8-6312-4b94-b114-a445ab7fb377&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dcb4a95&sv=2)

At **Theme settings** -> click **Product card** -> **Set up for Product Card** -> enable setting '**Show size variants**' to show the **Size option** on the product card.

Settings

Meaning

Text

Sets the text color of product size variants.

Background

Sets the background color of product size variants.

Borderr

Sets the border color of product size variants.

Text hover

Sets the text color of product size variants for hover state.

Background hover

Sets the background color of product size variants for hover state.

Border hover

Sets the border color of product size variants for hover state.

# Set up Advanced Mega Menu/ Drop Down Menu | Ella Documentation

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/set-up-advanced-mega-menu-drop-down-menu#how-to-create-multi-level-dropdown-menu)

How to create multi-level dropdown menu?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOOJpiBCUVVlgPRRaSi48%252F106.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8bb0af1-1c94-413a-a40a-2e90c60a348d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed44a2fa&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Navigation**.
    
2.  Click the title of your main menu.
    
3.  Choose one of the menu items to be the header for your drop-down menu, or add a new menu item to be the header. If you don't want the header to link to anything, then you can enter `#` in the **Link** field when you add the menu item.
    
4.  Add menu items to include in the new drop-down menu. Click **Add menu item**, enter the name of the menu item, and enter or select a destination for the link.
    
5.  Click and drag the menu items to nest below the header item.
    
6.  Click **Save menu**.
    

circle-info

For more information, see [Shopify Navigation Tutorial 2018 How to Create Drop Down Menusarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B_b0KEEa9sY)
.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/set-up-advanced-mega-menu-drop-down-menu#how-to-setup-mega-menu-layouts-advanced-mega-menu)

How to setup Mega menu layouts (Advanced Mega Menu)?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This video for Ella from version 6.0.0 to 6.4.0

1.  To show mega menu layouts, you need to [create multi-level dropdown menu](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/set-up-advanced-mega-menu-drop-down-menu#how-to-create-multi-level-dropdown-menu)
     first.
    
2.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
3.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
4.  In the **Header** section on the left editor window -> Click **\+ Add block**.
    
5.  Select block type is "**Mega Menu**".
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FDn28fpFNiTmNOhBzVc66%252Fmega-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da57ae9c6-886b-4631-9acf-e500ff14919e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85f30f32&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/set-up-advanced-mega-menu-drop-down-menu#put-the-name-of-collection-on-navigation-which-you-want-to-apply-mega-menu-layout-for-it-into-the-te)

Put the name of collection on navigation which you want to apply mega menu layout for it into the text box: Mega Menu Item

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FQZez8ukJEpbJn8sh7fsu%252F25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bc8b749-54ae-4fe1-8671-09b5051da2b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67442cd6&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F6arbvUnwmQ9XJzLCjGy7%252F110.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De91a3fca-aea7-4704-bf39-9a3c4fd145e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5cacdd07&sv=2)

# Typography | Ella Documentation

**Typography** allows setting the font elements such as font, font size, and alignment of texts for the site.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store ->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **Typography.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F7bsDrl9CJKjUHxJ4fuJ7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4fe79c7-d888-4129-ba6c-6d37b6655f0e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad150448&sv=2)

circle-info

Optimize your website's performance by utilizing shopify fonts! Selecting a different font can affect the speed of your store. [Learn more about system fonts.arrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/online-store/os/store-speed/improving-speed#fonts)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/typography#how-to-setup-google-font)

How to setup Google Font?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use hundreds of free, open-source fonts available through [Google Fontsarrow-up-right](http://fonts.google.com/)
.

1.  Search font.
    
2.  Copy name of font which you choose.
    
3.  At **Font source** setting -> select **Google fonts** option.
    
4.  Paste text which you have copied to **"Google font name"** setting.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRRhVae2B0l1g0ExagrlJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88a66c6d-606d-4f57-ad6c-98fc37db2657&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66552fb1&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwxJc2AhvOoApb4iBS9yv%252Ffont-family-2-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd74a1ba-97e9-404b-b644-ecc91a5f4afc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1829368&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/typography#how-to-setup-shopify-font)

How to setup Shopify Font?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Shopify's font library is a [collection of fontsarrow-up-right](https://shopify.dev/themes/architecture/settings/fonts#available-fonts)
 that includes system fonts, a selection of Google fonts, and licensed fonts from [Monotypearrow-up-right](https://www.monotype.com/)
. These fonts are free to use on all Shopify online stores, and are provided in both [WOFFarrow-up-right](https://caniuse.com/#feat=woff)
 and [WOFF2arrow-up-right](https://caniuse.com/#feat=woff2)
 formats.

1.  At **Font source** setting -> select **Shopify fonts** option.
    
2.  Click the **Change** button in the **Shopify font** setting to choose the font you want.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FnxG6LAD4JXRnTPCwHudU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16c67e48-ea71-4805-a863-ce39e8702d7e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6505345&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FSrhhPXwnubu9heGWAgla%252Ffont-family-2-1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08b7db0a-4a29-4bb0-b6e7-44c8482b8665&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6170d51&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/typography#body-font)

**Body font**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting

Description

Font family

Select a font family to apply to the body text:

*   **Font family #1**
    
*   **Font family #2**
    

Font size

Set the font size to apply to the body text ranging from 10px to 100px.

Font weight

Set the font weight to apply to the body text:

*   **Normal**
    
*   **Medium**
    
*   **Semi bold**
    
*   **Bold**
    
*   **Extra bold**
    
*   **Black**
    

Line height

Set the line height to apply to the body text.

Letter spacing

Set the spacing between letters to apply to the body text.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/typography#heading-font)

Setting

*   **Normal**
    
*   **Capitalize**
    
*   **Uppercase**
    
*   **Lowercase**
    

Line height

Set the line height to apply to headings and titles.

Letter spacing

Set the spacing between letters to apply to headings and titles.

Border height

Set the height of the border (underline) for headings and titles.

**Product quick view**

These settings are only applied when the **Quick View style** setting in **Product card** section is set to **Default**.

Setting

Description

Font size

Line height

Set the line height to apply to the product quick view.

Corner radius

Set the radius of the quick view button's corners. Can be from 0px to 50px, increasing arithmetically of 1px (pixel).

Top padding

Determines the height of the top inner space of the quick view button. Can be from 0px to 50px, increasing arithmetically of 1px (pixel).

Bottom padding

Determines the height of the bottom inner space of the quick view button. Can be from 0px to 50px, increasing arithmetically of 2px (pixel).

Left/Right padding

Determines the width of the left and right inner space of the quick view button. Can be from 0px to 50px, increasing arithmetically of 1px (pixel).

Show box shadow

Adds a shadow effect around the quick view button.

*   **Capitalize**
    
*   **Uppercase**
    
*   **Lowercase**
    

Line height

Set the line height to apply to the primary button.

Letter spacing

Set the spacing between letters to apply to the primary button.

Corner radius

Set the radius of the primary button's corners. Can be from 0px to 30px, increasing arithmetically of 1px (pixel).

Border width

Determines the thickness of the primary button borders. The range is from 0 to 30px.

Border style

Select the style for the primary button borders:

*   **Solid**
    
*   **Dotted**
    
*   **Dashed**
    

Show outline

Display an outline on the right and bottom of the primary button.

Text alignment

The alignment of the text within the primary button:

*   **Left** \- Aligns the text to the left.
    
*   **Center** \- Aligns the text in the center.
    
*   **Right** - Aligns the text to the right.
    

Top padding

Determines the spacing between the primary button text and its top border.

Bottom padding

Determines the spacing between the primary button text and its bottom border.

**Box shadow**

Setting

Description

Horizontal length

Determines how many pixels the box shadow falls horizontally.

Vertical length

Determines how many pixels the box shadow falls vertically.

Blur radius

Determines how blur the shadow is.

Spread

Determines how far the shadow keeps its original thickness from its origin.

Box shadow color

Set the color of the shadow.

Box shadow hover color

Set the color of the shadow when button is hovered.

Opacity

Fill in the desired transparency of the box shadow.

Inset shadow

Select whether the shadow will fall inside of button if YES or outside of button if NO.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/typography#secondary-button)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Description

*   **Font family #1**
    
*   **Font family #2**
    

Font size

Font weight

Set the font weight to apply to the secondary button:

*   **Normal**
    
*   **Medium**
    
*   **Semi bold**
    
*   **Bold**
    
*   **Extra bold**
    
*   **Black**

*   **Uppercase**
    
*   **Lowercase**

# Mobile Menu | Ella Documentation

Ella theme allows you to set up the menu on mobile and desktop separately.

Intro Video

Instruction Video

To set up the mobile menu, please follow instructions below:

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme Settings ->** **Multiple Layouts -> Menu Mobile Layout.**
    
4.  Choose **Layout Custom**. If you choose **Layout** **Default**, the desktop menu is applied.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FsIQTB63JxGxYOc0Y1B08%252Fmenu-mobile.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9847187-3f02-4a8e-a57e-275d079b3e80&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=daa103ec&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/mobile-menu#how-to-configure-mobile-menu)

How to configure Mobile Menu?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ella provides 3 Mobile menu tabs corresponding to 3 sections as shown below:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FDDaQb28f03STTcathWY1%252F117.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a16ddce-a724-4717-bb76-4b486d896ce0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a089f7e9&sv=2)

Each section has different menu blocks and you can add the type of block you want.

*   Menu Item
    
*   Link Item
    
*   Menu List
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F4nEHumE4R8tKsjlAAGFq%252F118.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e35c61b-d14b-4709-bfb3-cc65d4dbaf2e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=313a3043&sv=2)

circle-info

Note: Please fill out **Heading** text box of Mobile Menu. **The heading must be different for each mobile menu section.**

After adding the menu item, please reload Theme Editor View to see the change. You can check the change on actual devices like mobile or tablet.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOejxnYiqaScFIxQukzOm%252Fmenu-mobile-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ea63f23-f0c7-42c1-8f0e-f46024606f25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa00b6c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/mobile-menu#how-to-set-up-icon-image-for-mobile-menu)

How to set up icon / image for Mobile Menu?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/mobile-menu#menu-level-1)

Menu Level 1

You can set up icons or images for Menu Level 1:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FpTuToUP7tVEbqydI59X0%252Fmenu-mobile-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De59a0c33-749c-4a42-bc15-79e3c5584416&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b93c70a8&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FZnfCW56GaAd6Pp56yqB7%252Fmenu-mobile-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddda92564-4bf1-43ee-b19d-5ee0ebc8116f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=31575a7d&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FBBfp1JfgBw7i1HGCGKCf%252Fmenu-mobile-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc377b60b-7e77-45d1-b85e-3e21db2a88fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a5bc156&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/mobile-menu#menu-level-2-and-menu-level-3-list-layout)

Menu Level 2 & Menu Level 3 (List Layout)

About level 2, level 3 menu, you can set up images only:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FTQCJvtX5yk1rJzaFXTII%252Fmenu-mobile-7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D951ad689-5485-4bf0-8422-5f92b9917856&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50a41dc6&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FkDKJmRfIhCp4Os5gcxfO%252Fmenu-mobile-8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6230428d-e30a-4502-b067-9c98cc595a5a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e01857d4&sv=2)

circle-info

Upload image with the same name as the \[handle-of-menu\]\[menu-level-2-name\].\[IMG FORMAT\]

To get the image URL, please upload the image in **Settings** **\->** **Files**. Then copy the link. You can refer to [this linkarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/shopify-admin/productivity-tools/file-uploads)
.

Naming convention: lower cap and use "-" to replace white space. For example: with the menu level 2 "Top Rated" and menu handle "menu-mobile-new-in", the image name will be menu-mobile-new-intop-rated.jpg or menu-mobile-new-intop-rated.png

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/mobile-menu#menu-level-3-grid-layout)

Menu Level 3 (Grid Layout)

Please turn on "**Show Images Below The Sub Menu Items?"** checkbox to show **Grid Layout** for Menu Level 3:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FV6I4aoKPdQWK3uheKnfo%252Fmenu-mobile-9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db40a2dc1-979d-4b14-81cc-2f85c60531fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c32368eb&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FUa1tmpPlwj0KC5ZTLnXu%252Fmenu-mobile-10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab855213-8208-458f-9f5d-eaa0894bbb43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0dfbf1d&sv=2)

circle-info

Upload image with the same name as the \[handle-of-menu\]\[menu-level-3-name\].\[IMG FORMAT\]

To get the image URL, please upload the image in **Settings** **\->** **Files**. Then copy the link. You can refer to [this linkarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/shopify-admin/productivity-tools/file-uploads)
.

# General colors | Ella Documentation

Here you can change color for many elements on theme.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Click **Theme settings ->** **General colors.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#body)

Body

Settings

Meaning

Background

The background color of an entire page.

Background gradient

The background gradient of an entire page.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#placeholder)

Placeholder

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F1kLNkUwIJiQfqemZ1evp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd64ee1dc-6bcc-4b5e-abe6-068d77ecb935&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=98f9b110&sv=2)

Settings

Meaning

Background

Use as a placeholder background for loading images.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#warning)

Warning

Settings

Meaning

Text

The text color of the warning popup.

Background

The background color of the warning popup.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#text)

Text

Settings

Meaning

Default text

The default color of the text for an entire page.

It is applied to elements that have not been assigned a specific color.

Alternative text

The color of the alternative text.

It is being applied to elements:

*   Text on product compare popup
    
*   Text on compare color popup
    
*   Product title on Bundle section
    
*   Varinant name on sidecart
    
*   'Your cart is empty' or 'Secure Shopping Guarantee' text on cart page
    
*   Date text on '\[Sidebar\] Recent Post' block
    
*   .._._
    

Gray

Customize the text color of gray text.

It is being applied to elements:

*   Form message
    
*   'Tax included' text on side cart
    
*   Search trending and Placeholder text of search input on search popup
    
*   Variant name and product vendor of cart item on cart page.
    
*   'Coupon code' and 'Tax included' text on cart page.
    
*   ...
    

White

Customize the text color of white text.

It is being applied to elements:

*   Content text on Before You Leave popup
    
*   Close icon on the popups
    
*   Text on the color swatch's tooltip
    
*   Text on the cookie popup
    
*   Text of the count down block on product page
    
*   ...
    

Black

Customize the text color of black text. It is being applied to elements:

*   Close icon on the mobile menu
    
*   Background of close button on Filter Sidebar.
    
*   ...
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#link)

Link

Settings

Meaning

Text

The text color of the links on all pages.

Text hover

The text color of the links for hover state on all pages.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#breadcrumb)

Breadcrumb

Settings

Meaning

Text

The text color of the breadcrumb.

Text hover

The text color of the breadcrumb for hover state.

Text active

The text color of the breadcrumb for active state.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#alert)

Alert

Settings

Meaning

Error text

The color of the error text on the error alert popup.

Error background

The background of the error alert popup.

Success text

The color of the success text on the success alert popup.

Success background

The background of the error success popup.

Info text

The color of the info text on the info alert popup.

Info background

The background of the info success popup.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#global)

Global

Settings

Meaning

Text

This color is being applied to elements:

*   Background and border color of the product remove button on the compare product popup.
    
*   Background color of the Sticky Add To Cart Style 2 on mobile.
    
*   Background and border of the Style 1 count down block on product page
    
*   Text on pickup popup
    
*   Background of tooltip
    
*   ...
    

Border

This color is being applied to elements:

*   Background of the track of the scrollbar on the product combo list
    
*   Border top and border bottom the product combo item
    
*   ...
    

Background

This color is being applied to elements:

*   Background of the pages or articles in search results on the search page.
    
*   Background of the blockquote
    
*   ...
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/theme-settings/general-colors#arrows)

Arrows

Settings

Meaning

Text

The icon color of the arrow item.

Border

# Section On Every Page | Ella Documentation

Online Store 2.0 introduces a new JSON template format that lets you add new and existing sections to most pages in your theme, and add and remove sections from any page directly in the Shopify theme editor. This feature lets merchants personalize many more aspects of a store without relying on a developer. It also lets developers build maintainable themes with more modular components. For more information, see [Shopify 2.0arrow-up-right](https://shopify.dev/themes)
.

circle-info

Some core pages such as: Password page, Checkout page, Account page, Order page will **not support sections** on these pages due to the structure of Shopify.

To create page and add sections to every page you want, see [this link](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/page/how-to-create-a-page#how-to-create-a-page-template)
.

[PreviousHome 37 - Craft Beerchevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-37-craft-beer)
[NextAll Sections in Themechevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/sections/all-sections-in-theme)

Last updated 8 months ago

# Home 07 - Electronics | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwqsieGyKkPReanplV1FT%252Fheader-5-style2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4bdc6ab-f40f-456e-ad0b-be51243cb89d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ec54576&sv=2)

[Home 07 - Electronicsarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126841434)

Key Moments: [10:54arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=654s)
 Home 07 - Electronics

To setup Header Home 07 - Electronics, you need to add the **Header - Single-Line** and sections to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Single-Line** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header Nav - Vertical Menu** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F0ME1yFCB17g4U8kbqqHA%252Fheader-4-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcee6d369-076d-4f73-abc1-e8270c2088b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4c7e3f3&sv=2)

circle-info

Please disable Vertical Menu to show navigation like on **Home 07 - Electronics** header.

*   Click on **Menu** block of the **Header Nav - Vertical Menu** section.
    
*   Go to settings **VERTICAL MENU** -> **Vertical Menu** -> Select **None**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWjin0Mrlxy5BXXMNyA4Z%252Fheader-4-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8af32283-8776-4a48-bca0-7c7d4c0af445&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=51c29928&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-07-electronics#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 07 - Electronics, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-07-electronics#preset-for-header-home-07-electronics)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F455E9bEhZsK2Spf1Gv3S%252Fheader-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da212f304-4e45-4789-ab1e-e4d8b0d8f42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f6c792e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-07-electronics#preset-for-header-home-07-electronics)

Preset for **Header** Home 07 - Electronics


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Home 05 - Surfing | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F8Xuox7Ibq9KrzSECZfe1%252F43.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6039e16-ceba-4f0d-92bb-899f3ca58142&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d327918&sv=2)

[Home 05 - Surfingarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126775898)

Key Moments: [07:54arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=474s)
 Home 05 - Surfing

To setup Header Home 05 - Surfing, you need to add the **Header Nav - Utility** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Utility** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FI0qFaSvbiVhoPu1YyNnr%252Fheader-4-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dced4c4c0-f088-402d-9b01-19861b5edf27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85bbca3c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-05-surfing#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 05 - Surfing, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-05-surfing#preset-for-header-home-05-surfing)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F455E9bEhZsK2Spf1Gv3S%252Fheader-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da212f304-4e45-4789-ab1e-e4d8b0d8f42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f6c792e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-05-surfing#preset-for-header-home-05-surfing)

Preset for **Header** Home 05 - Surfing

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FoWwqsDJFROQm2nvxwUq8%252F45.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae126fd7-73bf-401d-9d2d-ca68c8e70fbf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1c986ba&sv=2)

[Home 13 - Winter Sportarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127267418)

Key Moments: [19:00arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=1140s)
 Home 13 - Winter Sport

To setup Header Home 13 - Winter Sport, you need to add the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FH2mp47OBZzyBFrSCibAq%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D280983a8-1039-4e05-a951-7b69407ea096&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9520c09&sv=2)

     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.

# Home 01 - Classic | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FNjPhteqqA4wtQ3tqvnHs%252Fheader-1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3b68a97-0dfb-4275-823a-22db9bf953f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87679941&sv=2)

[Home 01 - Classicarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)

Key moments: [00:16arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=16s)
 Home 01 - Classic

To setup Header Home 01 - Classic, you need to add the **Header - Classic** and **Header Nav - Plain** sections to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Classic** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header Nav - Plain** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FAs9iZuTGkbXGNvG9tj0h%252Fheader-1-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d8cb5a7-0361-44fa-a0e4-1148526307f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64b61ca6&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-01-classic#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 01 - Classic, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-01-classic#preset-for-header-home-01-classic)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F455E9bEhZsK2Spf1Gv3S%252Fheader-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da212f304-4e45-4789-ab1e-e4d8b0d8f42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f6c792e&sv=2)

# Home 08 - Large Catalogs | Ella Documentation

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-08-large-catalogs#style-1)

Style 1

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FhbeyjKSTreU62THI5Cvd%252Fheader-7.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9233e957-2496-439c-b081-8c3f4dab9482&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80cdf75f&sv=2)

[Home 08 - Large Catalogsarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126906970)

Key Moments: [12:47arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=767s)
 Home 08 - Large Catalogs

To setup Header Home 08 - Large Catalogs, you need to add the **Header - Advanced** and **Header Nav - Vertical Menu** sections to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Advanced** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header Nav - Vertical Menu** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5BNgyrkuVMpL0rvbz1RX%252Fheader-7-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01d78862-f678-4445-af36-9b431510d5ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb64f0b5&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Menu** block of the **Header Nav - Vertical Menu** section.
    
2.  Go to settings **VERTICAL MENU** -> **Vertical Menu** -> select **Style 2** and change color of text, link as you like.
    
3.  After then, change
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FKlTVn7uLnaLFNtfYsuhv%252Fhome-8-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd5d0129-261d-45a2-9e69-1b188792cef1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d0a7911&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-08-large-catalogs#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 08 - Large Catalogs, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-08-large-catalogs#preset-for-header-home-08-large-catalogs)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F455E9bEhZsK2Spf1Gv3S%252Fheader-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da212f304-4e45-4789-ab1e-e4d8b0d8f42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f6c792e&sv=2)

# Home 12 - Men Fashion | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fonx39stN9Exiexrf7vfw%252F44.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96e2a3b3-abf4-45d9-8c71-c21854ddc23b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1343c899&sv=2)

 Home 12 - Men Fashion

► To setup Header Home 12 - Men Fashion, you need to add the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FH2mp47OBZzyBFrSCibAq%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D280983a8-1039-4e05-a951-7b69407ea096&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9520c09&sv=2)

circle-info

To setup header transparent like header of **Home 12 - Men Fashion**:

1.  Click on the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section.
    
2.  Go to **TRANSPARENT HEADER** setting -> tick on the **Enable on homepage** checkbox
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRKN2nmV2xURzg8rpOt2y%252Fheader-9-setting-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabe4d477-92fb-4e2f-970a-a056a001ee41&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f18077dc&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FpkhfwGYeVwUE68BvFOum%252F47.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe6eba8d-b745-4359-bac5-df729b48aaea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd687db2&sv=2)

[Home 18 - Shoesarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123190444122)

Key Moments: [25:51arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=1551s)
 Home 18 - Shoes

To setup Header Home 18 - Shoes, you need to add the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FH2mp47OBZzyBFrSCibAq%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D280983a8-1039-4e05-a951-7b69407ea096&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9520c09&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-18-shoes#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 18 - Shoes, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-18-shoes#preset-for-header-home-18-shoes)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F455E9bEhZsK2Spf1Gv3S%252Fheader-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da212f304-4e45-4789-ab1e-e4d8b0d8f42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f6c792e&sv=2)
