# Home 09 - Pet Supplies | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fp10KAApCcfuGGt6zbTHu%252F52.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e4b6897-66fe-439c-a561-b7d45fd74692&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e00e1b&sv=2)

[Home 09 - Pet Suppliesarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127005274)

Key Moments: [14:32arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=872s)
 Home 09 - Pet Supplies

To setup Header Home 09 - Pet Supplies, you need to add the **Header - Single-Line** and **Header Nav - Plain** sections to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Single-Line** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header Nav - Plain** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FxKo30cnwWxEy0NL6qjXn%252Fheader-6-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df55c2adf-310b-4609-8be9-c6cf93f4f1e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ecd4e06&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-09-pet-supplies#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 09 - Pet Supplies, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-09-pet-supplies#preset-for-header-home-09-pet-supplies)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F455E9bEhZsK2Spf1Gv3S%252Fheader-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da212f304-4e45-4789-ab1e-e4d8b0d8f42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f6c792e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-09-pet-supplies#preset-for-header-home-09-pet-supplies)

Preset for **Header** Home 09 - Pet Supplies


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Home 06 - SuperMarket | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FiOFS8IrHNEj0rEVwTDko%252Fheader-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df64ac736-2caa-452e-8c49-bc9f36dd4312&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da500a10&sv=2)

[Home 06 - SuperMarketarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126808666)

Key Moments: [08:46arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=526s)
 Home 06 - SuperMarket

To setup Header Home 06 - SuperMarket, you need to add the **Header - Single-Line** and sections to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Single-Line** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header Nav - Vertical Menu** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F0ME1yFCB17g4U8kbqqHA%252Fheader-4-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcee6d369-076d-4f73-abc1-e8270c2088b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4c7e3f3&sv=2)

circle-info

To show vertical menu of **Home 06 - SuperMarket** like on theme demo:

*   Click on **Menu** block of the **Header Nav - Vertical Menu** section.
    
*   Go to **VERTICAL MENU** setting -> **Vertical Menu** -> Select **Style 3** and change color of text, icon,..in
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F3Wnoc4Xae30l312hxdHq%252Fheader-4-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b3c689a-b8d4-4d2d-be4c-ec1d4ccf3294&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27b941ca&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-06-supermarket#to-show-icons-for-vertical-menu-please-follow-our-instruction-below)

To show icons for vertical menu, please follow our instruction below:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FI4oL0u1mUmkuRvAKMk3D%252F121.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D298db3f2-ac27-459e-ae75-0e5df1e6867a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2957a9d9&sv=2)

*   Create a Menu in **Navigation** for Vertical menu. **Remember the name of each collection in the menu level 01**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvRwvZcwVoscb08dSG0O6%252F122.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D178f4327-a4bf-4536-950d-62733ff32408&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c3680140&sv=2)

1.  Prepare an image of the icon you want. Name it with the same name as **the collection in the menu level 01** (please use **PNG** image).
    
2.  You need to go to **Settings** --> **Files**, upload images here
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FaakSjoKogkUJ5OPtfSxl%252F123.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0c84fab-ea90-4e40-a31d-733af3e40a38&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=deeabf33&sv=2)

circle-info

Rules: Lower cap and use a hyphen "-" to replace white space if your image name has the white space. **For example:** with the menu name "Electronics" the image name will be **electronics.png**

circle-exclamation

Recommended size for icon image: 20 x 20px

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-06-supermarket#upload-settings-for-header)

# Home 02 - Trendy Style | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FsRXtesWoBZ7OAMcFyLjY%252F100.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Decf08fcb-c036-45c1-9055-e4d799244b1d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8eadb134&sv=2)

[Home 02 - Trendy stylearrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126317146)

Key moments: [02:01arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=121s)
 Home 02 - Trendy Style

To setup Header Home 02 - Trendy Style, you need to add the **Header Nav - Multi Site** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Multi Site** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FCmmsnMGWP5ywtLBiH7ZH%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd57b2e3-1e87-4e8c-8c7f-14d190f1732c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35c1d86b&sv=2)

circle-info

You can show menu tabs: Women, Men, Kids like on theme demo by using **Menu Tab** block.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FyV0kdDcaPQ5sJc7rKyvR%252Fheader-2b-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31d619e7-0f60-44a1-862e-6861f66ffa9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=244badc4&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5Ml6om78VmfHUVHDrUcd%252Fheader-2-menu-tab-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19dda247-ccd5-45b7-a091-5040c95a6129&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=975ee0&sv=2)

circle-info

The first tab "ELLA" is Homepage, you don't need to choose link for this tab, the other tabs are [**Landing Page**arrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~/changes/ya8CSeFxwPyu94dBt1WL/page/landing-page)
 and will link to the page you created.

With this header, there are 2 steps to set up:

*   Create Landing page
    
*   Set up different menu for each Landing Page
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-02-trendy-style#how-to-set-up-different-navigation-menu-for-tabs)

How to set up different navigation/menu for tabs?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Navigation.**
    
2.  Click **Add menu** to create a menu you want to use for menu tab.
    
3.  Go to the landing page you created to activate menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fp7dmnIVxsVl8ldZLuWSU%252Fmenu-tab-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34aa1aaa-8651-47dc-9919-6047b20dbb21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22824432&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FsE8OduRIvO9NHzUpWp5K%252Fmenu-tab-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc82685db-69d3-4c91-9380-63ed7c5a77b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7b0985a&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FUkyrjZOvu2YcUrZtZ1ej%252Fmenu-tab-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bf0306c-a11d-4c50-af90-5ebb60d4fd55&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2566df4&sv=2)

circle-info

The selected template must contain the word 'landing'. For example: template\_landing.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FNQVaJrQpVRgcHae0NjEX%252Fmenu-tab-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9547142-2ea0-4c92-b9d0-256562125c53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a281c938&sv=2)

circle-info

URL and Handle of Landing pages must be the same as the handle that you created in the navigation above.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-02-trendy-style#upload-settings-for-header)

# Home 23 - Plant+ Garden | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F4veH7fbS9SIjco2XkAXu%252Fheader-13.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f86f39b-77af-4a31-b309-ca98b11d120c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4dc3b644&sv=2)

[Home 23 - Plant+ Gardenarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=124314517555)

Key Moments: [31:53arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=1913s)
 Home 23 - Plant+ Garden

To setup Header Home 23 - Plant+ Garden, you need to add the **Header Nav - Utility** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Utility** section.

Upload Settings For Header


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 23 - Plant+ Garden, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-23-plant+-garden#preset-for-header-home-23-plant+-garden)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.

3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**

# Home 04 - High Fashion | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fs8hKYaLqvSvKK70xUIG4%252F99.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc0e0fef-7cd9-4fa0-902e-1c2926b2b162&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9db00251&sv=2)

[Home 04 - High Fashionarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126710362)

Key Moments: [05:32arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=332s)
 Home 04 - High Fashion

To setup header for Home 04 - High Fashion, you need to add the **Header Nav - Multi Site** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Multi Site** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FCmmsnMGWP5ywtLBiH7ZH%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd57b2e3-1e87-4e8c-8c7f-14d190f1732c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35c1d86b&sv=2)

circle-info

You can show menu tabs: Women, Men, Kids like on theme demo by using **Menu Tab** block.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FyV0kdDcaPQ5sJc7rKyvR%252Fheader-2b-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31d619e7-0f60-44a1-862e-6861f66ffa9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=244badc4&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5Ml6om78VmfHUVHDrUcd%252Fheader-2-menu-tab-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19dda247-ccd5-45b7-a091-5040c95a6129&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=975ee0&sv=2)

circle-info

The first tab "ELLA" is Homepage, you don't need to choose link for this tab, the other tabs are [**Landing Page**arrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~/changes/ya8CSeFxwPyu94dBt1WL/page/landing-page)
 and will link to the page you created.

With this header, there are 2 steps to set up:

*   Create Landing page
    
*   Set up different menu for each Landing Page
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-04-high-fashion#how-to-set-up-different-navigation-menu-for-tabs)

How to set up different navigation/menu for tabs?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Navigation.**
    
2.  Click **Add menu** to create a menu you want to use for menu tab.
    
3.  Go to the landing page you created to activate menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fp7dmnIVxsVl8ldZLuWSU%252Fmenu-tab-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34aa1aaa-8651-47dc-9919-6047b20dbb21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22824432&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FsE8OduRIvO9NHzUpWp5K%252Fmenu-tab-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc82685db-69d3-4c91-9380-63ed7c5a77b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7b0985a&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FUkyrjZOvu2YcUrZtZ1ej%252Fmenu-tab-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bf0306c-a11d-4c50-af90-5ebb60d4fd55&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2566df4&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FNQVaJrQpVRgcHae0NjEX%252Fmenu-tab-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9547142-2ea0-4c92-b9d0-256562125c53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a281c938&sv=2)

circle-info

URL and Handle of Landing pages must be the same as the handle that you created in the navigation above.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-16-game#preset-for-header-home-16-game)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.

4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.

Key Moments: [19:45arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=1185s)
 Home 14 - Automotive 1

To setup Header Home 14 - Automotive 1, you need to add the **Header - Single-Line** and **Header Nav - Plain** sections to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Single-Line** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header Nav - Plain** section to add.

3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.

 Home 26- Bagratica

To setup Header Home 26- Bagratica, you need to add the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FH2mp47OBZzyBFrSCibAq%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D280983a8-1039-4e05-a951-7b69407ea096&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9520c09&sv=2)

1.  On the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section settings -> **Header Style** \-> select **Balance both sides by logo**.

# Quick Order List | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FQBfhogODiLt98GfRYW5u%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23b4d37e-40ee-4ed5-ac7f-00cfd8fb4859&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6424c429&sv=2)

The **Quick Order List** function in Shopify allows customers to easily purchase multiple product quantities and variants in bulk, enhancing the shopping experience for B2B or wholesale buyers.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Products** from the dropdown window.
    
4.  Click **Product information ->** scroll down to **Quick order list**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FjHvKQru5xMU2rJMeJhqI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39b22c40-b33e-4ba8-b36d-782cfa1edf43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=349983ae&sv=2)

Settings

Meaning

Show quick order list

Enable to show quick order list function.

Show images

Shows images of variations.

Show SKUs

Shows SKUs of variations.

[PreviousProduct Combochevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo)
[NextProduct Description Tabchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-description-tab)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Home 24 - Bicycle | Ella Documentation

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-24-bicycle#style-balance-both-sides-by-menu)

Style: Balance both sides by menu

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FVrf2ELBe6Jz0ZeY9icro%252Fheader-14.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D383b5364-9872-4445-8302-fb8f642db1c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b7af31e&sv=2)

[Home 24 - Bicyclearrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=124314583091)

Key Moments: [33:01arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=1981s)
 Home 24 - Bicycle

To setup Header Home 24 - Bicycle, you need to add the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FH2mp47OBZzyBFrSCibAq%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D280983a8-1039-4e05-a951-7b69407ea096&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9520c09&sv=2)

1.  On the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section settings -> **Header Style** \-> select **Balance both sides by menu**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FedX5TLE0fhQT5TVq9TLm%252Fnav-hamburger-style.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8067339-d8d2-4637-9632-9306871cff9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c60a51c7&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Header Icons** block -> you can select icon for Search, Account, Wishlist, Cart and Languge / Currency -> select **Bold** at the **Icon Style** setting.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F0a2ci8Zmk3P5FPnf5rO3%252Fnav-hamburger-header-icons.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dded02449-a04d-45ca-b6b1-15f5e441ed38&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d4ef4b7&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-24-bicycle#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 24 - Bicycle, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-24-bicycle#preset-for-header-home-24-bicycle)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F455E9bEhZsK2Spf1Gv3S%252Fheader-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da212f304-4e45-4789-ab1e-e4d8b0d8f42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f6c792e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-24-bicycle#preset-for-header-home-24-bicycle)

Preset for **Header** Home 24 - Bicycle


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up the header for **Home 32 - Suitcase**, you need to add the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section to the HEADER GROUP.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.

4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section.

# Home 19 - Swimwear 1 | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FfTAQ2jsSb18CTDgouVAx%252Fheader-8-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b313001-6a8d-4db9-b4b1-cbf67148250c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9ad9423&sv=2)

[Home 19 - Swimwear 1arrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123360739379)

Key Moments: [26:38arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=1598s)
 Home 19 - Swimwear 1

To setup Header Home 19 - Swimwear 1, you need to add the **Header - Basic** and **Header Nav - Plain** sections to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Basic** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header Nav - Plain** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FZOXxnqZelJqGww8PdeUv%252Fheader-8-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De349cf72-1aeb-4e1e-b5b6-f654b88cfb03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d3bf410&sv=2)

circle-info

To setup header transparent like header of **Home 19 - Swimwear 1**:

1.  Click on the **Header Basic** section.
    
2.  Go to **TRANSPARENT HEADER** setting -> tick on the **Enable on homepage** checkbox
    
3.  Same for **Header Nav - Plain** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FKmL4Ct3S8ITgRbDkv34k%252Fheader-8-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e9b2302-124e-4875-a3d8-54c1eba8d228&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ef819b7&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F05gOSoBjmrPxvNSLgu52%252Fheader-8-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd6acb13-e529-4220-a291-66acc689dff9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b34136fd&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-19-swimwear-1#upload-settings-for-header)

# Home 33 - Coffee Shop | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FoZuzUju1QrbesNJPlSJT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33a04117-f878-4cba-b188-613071159c23&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a3dc032&sv=2)

To set up header for **Home 33 - Coffee Shop**, you need to add the **Header - Advanced** and **Header nav - hamburger slide-in** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header - Advanced** section.
    
5.  Same for **Header nav - hamburger slide-in** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FTeCzplylsEk4YPtgzkkF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1cf8e90-6c61-4501-8191-28460dba2cdc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99a9ded9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-33-coffee-shop#upload-settings-for-header)

Upload Settings For Header


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Header Home 33 - Coffee Shop, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to download](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-33-coffee-shop#preset-for-home-33-coffee-shop)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.

4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **header-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.

# Home 28 - Single Product | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FXFufNxiW9ugT8v9bsqmD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd7fb2e14-a608-4749-b71c-0e1e2f94129c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28f354e8&sv=2)

To setup Header Home 28 - Single Product, you need to add the **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Hamburger Slide-In** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FgEHF4TJdeC3dI29SaKgz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6d67671-5310-4455-9959-4348efca9c97&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=768886ee&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Ffza6e94IAAqxBPJRhVzS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13b525af-af8c-4190-8d4c-55b536d5c457&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c60096c2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-28-single-product#set-up-a-scroll-to-row-anchor-single-page-menu-on-your-site)

Set up a scroll to row anchor (single page menu) on your site


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Navigation**.
    
2.  Find the menu that you want to edit.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FpDnihECZRk3i0DDnHnW3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc63b709b-7bfb-4963-88ee-74d01e50413f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3e0c151&sv=2)

1.  Select Menu Item and enter the Section ID name.
    

For example: #features

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F1DxKgvKvg49ZMIYE6nF5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74d76ea1-9c98-4f7d-a5e8-34cb195e18dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50854844&sv=2)

1.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
2.  Select Section and enter an ID name that matches the ID name you just entered for the Menu Item.
    

For example: features

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FZ7BIKUPnGPDqwBmSjaT8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1680e988-6168-459d-95c8-6808af1b9312&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c6abf5e&sv=2)

Note: If you include a link after #ID, clicking on the Menu will take you to the page where you attached the link and automatically scroll down to the corresponding section if one exists.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Ft4c0R0DXWlz0dwOldhnH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec28d63a-1812-4ed4-9062-380316e1ea05&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e159eb32&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F8rQhEw7Bhch7cThEeXW1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4b9bdea-048c-4bb7-89a2-7545088a6d35&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f9a71cd&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FIc869VmekGuSEsin4J5s%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea768a9c-dd9a-451e-ae67-402f8a8e0acf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f072cfcc&sv=2)

# Home 01 - Classic | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FAHJyUebBQ78tXG3eYJWS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46b1e62d-5613-4971-9ab3-0399860d4efa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d59590bc&sv=2)

[Home 01 - Classicarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127857242)

► To setup Footer Home 01 - Classic, you need to add the **Footer 01** section to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FgGFJBedBwv4skoz5IvOM%252Ffooter-1-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14fc1e5d-f16d-44fe-afb5-cd1d6a816392&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=720ab299&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

*   The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFEFZPuDqAHwkciCpLAh3%252Ffooter-1-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D510f35e2-1aec-4beb-93dd-4e8ba664fe4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=892c3872&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FN8LSpp6U2Os3V1USXtDj%252Ffooter-1-setting-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D942496f4-32d7-439f-b66e-6b8acf106f7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=982bf192&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWTqd4vCeg8r2APFaz9mp%252Ffooter-1-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4b426e-83e7-42fd-a3e1-be68fbb23f60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=486960e1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-01-classic#upload-settings-for-footer)

# Home 04 - High Fashion | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPi43Av4zsVNbPsLFmUPL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D178a75fe-78d8-4a8c-a4d6-545112801d53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c65b11a&sv=2)

To setup Footer Layout 04, you need to add the **Footer 04** section to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 04** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F6EFRPaK4QYaxWN2hVnaH%252Ffooter-4-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D314f3594-d531-4a26-b287-71a6c36a18d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f21a1591&sv=2)

In the **Footer 04** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 1. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FVD2sfQDwViCVvVBS7mgi%252Ffooter-4-text.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb284edc-090c-4ad0-834a-4dc3bf4417bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7d717d&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 3. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FLtrrknr5tQvEpQvzfNQ9%252Ffooter-4-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7921103-b11a-4655-95aa-cd43c854add7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7be57da1&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    
    *   The settings are for the block width, title, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
        
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FJyNyOinFxh4pP5rWYdea%252Ffooter-4-newsletter.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafc27a8a-5ef2-448d-ae2e-f780963faa5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e266fc56&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F3DgqLblgQ3YqatxSDr2j%252Ffooter-4-social.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc24c16e8-c06e-4253-9732-063f111ba8ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12f37587&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPgmRR2dxFOcNu9K2h5Tz%252Ffooter-4-bottom-copyright.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75c405af-a9f3-4486-a4fa-203257c68b3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=479ebb5&sv=2)

Upload Settings For Footer


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 04 - High Fashion, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-04-high-fashion#preset-for-footer-home-04-high-fashion)
     [arrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/ag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi/~/changes/453/footer/new-footer-section-group-layout/layout-01#preset-for-footer-layout-01)
    the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRPtqwgG6ABSZWhqME4z6%252Ffooter-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3b1071-06c8-4f29-b2cb-cf36a84c9363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9f9ffab&sv=2)

# Home 03 - In vogue | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FN5qhD1aCgiXv5CiYI1d8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05267bcb-6f45-4824-aa1f-de221de5ad02&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a21eed1b&sv=2)

[Home 03 - In voguearrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126677594)

To setup Footer Layout 03, you need to add the **Newsletter** and **Footer 03** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Newsletter** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 03** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F7PiWgioUU72LzGdMtDLd%252Ffooter-3-add-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57923394-b878-4e1c-b453-e769aa5e6cc8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=560fa27a&sv=2)

► In the **Newsletter** section settings. Add or adjust **Newsletter** block as your need:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FEjAvWb5lNltTie0N0aeQ%252Fnewsletter-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4da0b886-f414-45b5-b7e4-006db555002d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1aeaac2&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 03** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 3. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FJL1WOx9cHAD4xwoG5Rr5%252Ffooter-3-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42ff01cc-6ecc-40c4-b993-b69ab0f2c8df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f34b5d0&sv=2)

1.  **Social With Payment** block: Limit 1. The settings consist of two components: Social Media Icons and Payment. The social component allows you to change the color, icon size, background, spacing between items, or even the static color associated for each item. The payment component is toggleable with settings for title and payment types, methods.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FS7nfAl1z4n0b5LEU1e79%252Ffooter-3-social.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4b74abc-44b5-4757-b41d-a63e1ed3070e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96eb2003&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FbuyJrqRLamgvDrEstEmy%252Ffooter-3-payment.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d0c771d-f2ce-45cc-9386-c445c1c56277&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4bd01507&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFuwJ3NiRrfDXjHH02l5l%252Ffooter-3-footer-bottom.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6ecd2b1-8bd0-492a-b56e-a73745ca94a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86c5f72e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-03-in-vogue#upload-settings-for-footer)

# Home 17 - Gym | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FrNSp1x8wLL5kEjtFBUdy%252Fheader-02-Style-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De223aae7-e0d7-4877-b156-e1cf492299fc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff74834b&sv=2)

[Home 17 - Gymarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127464026)

Key Moments: [24:01arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QJOSOCm7GuY&t=1441s)
 Home 17 - Gym

To setup Header Home 17 - Gym, you need to add the **Header Nav - Multi Site** section to the **HEADER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **HEADER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Header Nav - Multi Site** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FCmmsnMGWP5ywtLBiH7ZH%252Fheader-2-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd57b2e3-1e87-4e8c-8c7f-14d190f1732c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35c1d86b&sv=2)

1.  On the **Header Nav - Multi Site** section settings -> **Header Style ->** Select **Style 2**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Flhal7mT8FXjcfDm7LBK0%252Fhome-17-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D475eae11-ad08-4232-a49b-bdd7d3de2eb9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26ce97df&sv=2)

circle-info

You can show menu tabs: Women, Men, Kids like on theme demo by using **Menu Tab** block.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FyV0kdDcaPQ5sJc7rKyvR%252Fheader-2b-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31d619e7-0f60-44a1-862e-6861f66ffa9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=244badc4&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5Ml6om78VmfHUVHDrUcd%252Fheader-2-menu-tab-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19dda247-ccd5-45b7-a091-5040c95a6129&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=975ee0&sv=2)

circle-info

The first tab "ELLA" is Homepage, you don't need to choose link for this tab, the other tabs are [**Landing Page**arrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~/changes/ya8CSeFxwPyu94dBt1WL/page/landing-page)
 and will link to the page you created.

With this header, there are 2 steps to set up:

*   Create Landing page
    
*   Set up different menu for each Landing Page
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-17-gym#how-to-set-up-different-navigation-menu-for-tabs)

How to set up different navigation/menu for tabs?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Navigation.**
    
2.  Click **Add menu** to create a menu you want to use for menu tab.
    
3.  Go to the landing page you created to activate menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fp7dmnIVxsVl8ldZLuWSU%252Fmenu-tab-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34aa1aaa-8651-47dc-9919-6047b20dbb21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22824432&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FsE8OduRIvO9NHzUpWp5K%252Fmenu-tab-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc82685db-69d3-4c91-9380-63ed7c5a77b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7b0985a&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FUkyrjZOvu2YcUrZtZ1ej%252Fmenu-tab-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bf0306c-a11d-4c50-af90-5ebb60d4fd55&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2566df4&sv=2)

circle-info

The selected template must contain the word 'landing'. For example: template\_landing.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FNQVaJrQpVRgcHae0NjEX%252Fmenu-tab-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9547142-2ea0-4c92-b9d0-256562125c53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a281c938&sv=2)

circle-info

URL and Handle of Landing pages must be the same as the handle that you created in the navigation above.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/header/header-for-desktop/home-17-gym#upload-settings-for-header)

# Home 02 - Trendy Style | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FgsKStsHeMoNbk9Qt8mgJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f8de4fc-c152-4d64-ac1a-c7c6962add82&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d899b0c&sv=2)

[Home 02 - Trendy Stylearrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126317146)

To setup Footer Home 02 - Trendy Style, you need to add the **Footer 02** section to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 02** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FL7eI3Kac5LjtPG7VCUJp%252Ffooter-10-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca9ede81-6cf1-441e-8290-54c2dd20aa2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcf34895&sv=2)

In the **Footer 02** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    
    *   The settings are for the block width, title, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
        
    *   To show newsletter like on Home 02 - Trendy Style demo -> go to setting **Style Layout** \-> select **Style 2**.
        
        ![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fu6jzIKUqe61J7Zt3h7GW%252Ffooter-2-style.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac5e240f-9a3b-4e85-ab20-7e9964148f5e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b4803f6&sv=2)
        
    *   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons.
        
    
    ![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FG153wmRgtmGHD0Nc0Adc%252Ffooter-2-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf2ea6c2-99bc-4acc-b154-b05a96a1cd26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86fa57ae&sv=2)
    
    *   The block also allows the border right enabling to separate itself from other block such as text or menu.
        
    
    ![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FxUOPtjLm67FgQwvnQxP4%252Ffooter-2-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32526c37-f6c5-48f1-ab2f-2d0240ed2309&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56fe5204&sv=2)
    
2.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvHQLpfLSzhMz3HFSkXYS%252Ffooter-10-setting-footer-bottom.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68f2d209-1fc4-4280-bf30-b1981be75f18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a3d153c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-02-trendy-style#upload-settings-for-footer)

Upload Settings For Footer


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 02 - Trendy Style, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-02-trendy-style#preset-for-footer-home-02-trendy-style)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRPtqwgG6ABSZWhqME4z6%252Ffooter-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3b1071-06c8-4f29-b2cb-cf36a84c9363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9f9ffab&sv=2)

# Demo & Settings Data | Ella Documentation

To set up data for Collections list Layouts, please follow below instruction:

1.  Please click the [file to download](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-list-page/demo-and-settings-data#presets-for-collections-list)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want.
    
2.  Open downloaded file in the text editor.
    
3.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
4.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes ->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
5.  Find folder **Templates** **\->** Open file **list-collections.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE**. **PASTE** the copied preset from external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F7j8hvG69SzNLcZ0VzmfC%252F26.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09a463dc-ff9a-4d64-b5c5-22d9cf407d98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6a408dc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-list-page/demo-and-settings-data#collections-list-demo)

# Home 08 - Large Catalogs | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FHy2tAiSnPEWfGTG1EmDS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72d81b74-2bca-4d9a-bfff-80e73e5fbb5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fcd7191&sv=2)

To setup Home 08 - Large Catalogs, you need to add the **Newsletter** and **Footer 05** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Newsletter** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 05** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FylA8vZag99NsOce3l1Wf%252Ffooter-6-add-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4ee4d38-3fb5-4c93-ab6f-2f874599ac11&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b27d5a3&sv=2)

► In the **Newsletter** section settings. Add or adjust **Newsletter** block as your need:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FoA9sfQ3C3CyxPVLANYO2%252Ffooter-6-newsletter-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D280a2c7f-fec4-40cc-a587-e101f58a557e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfd4b235&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 05** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FAK8OsIMzUY5oQldWU7DY%252Ffooter-6-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D592c43d5-d6de-492f-964f-a41c7130fbbe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4896901&sv=2)

1.  **Text** block: Limit 1. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwvKVo5qpP8K9n9ujZHDm%252Ffooter-6-text.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80a9a7a8-4a3b-41db-8f85-31101979ba53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46ef086e&sv=2)

1.  **Security trust** block: Limit 1. The settings are simply for choosing image for trust guarantee.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FlSThfCm6VQpWWeDJNUl3%252Ffooter-6-security.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df87abcf9-5312-48e8-83d9-60e8b1bbaac7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffe5da91&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom**: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FxOrSUeyMy9C2iQ2yYJbZ%252Ffooter-6-bottom-copyright.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08c0d48a-3a6c-47b1-b412-33e2e434a7ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=287a75c1&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FW2cmr0Hxvi1iou6ajjsj%252Ffooter-6-bottom-payment.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6682a2f2-3571-4578-9cfa-db66a8246c4e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1152d4b1&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 05** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FAK8OsIMzUY5oQldWU7DY%252Ffooter-6-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D592c43d5-d6de-492f-964f-a41c7130fbbe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4896901&sv=2)

1.  **Text** block: Limit 1. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwvKVo5qpP8K9n9ujZHDm%252Ffooter-6-text.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80a9a7a8-4a3b-41db-8f85-31101979ba53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46ef086e&sv=2)

1.  **Security trust** block: Limit 1. The settings are simply for choosing image for trust guarantee.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FlSThfCm6VQpWWeDJNUl3%252Ffooter-6-security.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df87abcf9-5312-48e8-83d9-60e8b1bbaac7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffe5da91&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom**: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FxOrSUeyMy9C2iQ2yYJbZ%252Ffooter-6-bottom-copyright.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08c0d48a-3a6c-47b1-b412-33e2e434a7ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=287a75c1&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FW2cmr0Hxvi1iou6ajjsj%252Ffooter-6-bottom-payment.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6682a2f2-3571-4578-9cfa-db66a8246c4e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1152d4b1&sv=2)

# Sub Collection | Ella Documentation

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Collection** from the dropdown window.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FNsPGKtCqQesnatGEfW1V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b4612c1-0000-4d74-a2ce-adee30215bfd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1cbde5d4&sv=2)

4\. From Collection Header, Choose **"Add Block" -> Collection Description**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FL6aEnxnd2qPD3vTfjagN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9fc8ed89-b35c-40e1-b321-c114ead06fb0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=954e9c32&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FG9SzuL0f6Gzh4PW7LYav%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2519582-540c-4beb-89bc-14b54364be68&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd13d081&sv=2)

5\. From your Shopify admin, go to **Products** **\->** **Collections.**

6\. Find the **Collection** you want to show **Sub Collection**, and copy the name **Collection**.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FZDB5rbITrI6Qdhr1bxhl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1939da10-09eb-4c9b-b973-9cee273ffa8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0014fd8&sv=2)

7\. From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store->** **Navigation**, create a menu and paste the name of the collection just copied.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fe4YeDbPNKQ8eWtyrnecW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b8d5b5f-540a-43bf-b25a-ea1e64987fd2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7d9f4b2&sv=2)

8\. After adding the sub collection menu Item you go back to the **Collection** view to go out of the page to see it.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWtJry9Z0VFeZZjZC69li%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a8e05e9-5239-4a96-8f60-1d6e481b5e32&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a43e2739&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FnuFyF3rqnKIrKepFqguK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e369b5f-6e99-4819-9d79-fbd09a4fe71e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e766e9bb&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/sub-collection#in-addition-you-want-to-display-the-image-in-the-sub-collection-you-do-the-following)

In addition, you want to display the image in the sub collection you do the following.

1\. From your Shopify admin, go to **Products** **\->** **Collections**.

2\. Find the theme that you want to edit, and add pictures to the **Collection.**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FJ68S5I3NRBffec3epRFr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D12a9ed80-2bf8-41a2-94a7-f0497f7b2a49&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=290f6dd4&sv=2)

4\. From Collection Header, Choose **Collection Description**, and click "**Show Sub Collection Image?**".

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F0TSjB3cVmdeM1Ek8wYdO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1e0f307-b7b7-439f-a8a8-72f7013f58c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8aad5a50&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FgTk5eNYRpMI3r27u2h56%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbeb7b34b-01ab-4c76-96ee-305bc73db5b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25690647&sv=2)

# Demo & Settings Data | Ella Documentation

To set up data for Collection Layouts, please follow below instruction:

1.  Please click the [file to download](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/demo-and-settings-data#presets-for-collection)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want.
    
2.  Open downloaded file in the text editor.
    
3.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
4.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes ->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
5.  Find folder **Templates** **\->** Open file **collection.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE**. **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FeV3X8uUmcU4vBM0Z5D72%252F1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62069121-808d-4853-b848-afdab1e075b3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4fe2a55&sv=2)

# Home 05 - Surfing | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FEbRaKDYNi5MUj8bvFFyI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D294ec387-7bb1-4417-a64a-50a581177070&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3457024b&sv=2)

[Home 05 - Surfingarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123126775898)

► To setup Footer Home 05 - Surfing, you need to add the **Brand Slider** and **Footer 01** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Brands Slider** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 01** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FMy4P8pdOQ7dzJcpIqsWl%252Ffooter-1-setting-6.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30b3771f-ae05-4fc8-a1ec-0245004b58d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd15be3d&sv=2)

► In the **Brands Slider** section settings. Add or adjust **Image** blocks as your need.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fim1OrOhWICjh6fmPNqzd%252Ffooter-1-setting-7.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc710ed6d-0639-4a47-aea2-f37ec13d903b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8d540412&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 2. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5TrZeqaIO3PZ351i9WKs%252Ffooter-1-setting-8.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24ac04bb-bbf1-4e9a-96af-dc50509c506b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6aa37d5&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

*   The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFEFZPuDqAHwkciCpLAh3%252Ffooter-1-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D510f35e2-1aec-4beb-93dd-4e8ba664fe4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=892c3872&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FN8LSpp6U2Os3V1USXtDj%252Ffooter-1-setting-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D942496f4-32d7-439f-b66e-6b8acf106f7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=982bf192&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
