Upload Settings For Footer


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 05 - Surfing, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-05-surfing#preset-for-footer-home-05-surfing)
     [arrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/ag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi/~/changes/453/footer/new-footer-section-group-layout/layout-01#preset-for-footer-layout-01)
    the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRPtqwgG6ABSZWhqME4z6%252Ffooter-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3b1071-06c8-4f29-b2cb-cf36a84c9363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9f9ffab&sv=2)

# Home 12 - Men Fashion | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FrUy2o8ksKBENmME2OEj4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14988886-cb6a-4256-9715-957590d2f461&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7ff12a1&sv=2)

[Home 12 - Men Fashionarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127234650)

To setup Footer Layout 03, you need to add the **Newsletter** and **Footer 03** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Newsletter** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 03** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F7PiWgioUU72LzGdMtDLd%252Ffooter-3-add-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57923394-b878-4e1c-b453-e769aa5e6cc8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=560fa27a&sv=2)

► In the **Newsletter** section settings. Add or adjust **Newsletter** block as your need:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FkBsxcEggKeG6QHrtvSWp%252Ffooter-12-newsletter.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84881eee-e3c6-42e9-bd1a-1fff0bdd67ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77fda4d3&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 03** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 3. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FJL1WOx9cHAD4xwoG5Rr5%252Ffooter-3-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42ff01cc-6ecc-40c4-b993-b69ab0f2c8df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f34b5d0&sv=2)

1.  **Social With Payment** block: Limit 1. The settings consist of two components: Social Media Icons and Payment. The social component allows you to change the color, icon size, background, spacing between items, or even the static color associated for each item. The payment component is toggleable with settings for title and payment types, methods.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FS7nfAl1z4n0b5LEU1e79%252Ffooter-3-social.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4b74abc-44b5-4757-b41d-a63e1ed3070e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96eb2003&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FbuyJrqRLamgvDrEstEmy%252Ffooter-3-payment.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d0c771d-f2ce-45cc-9386-c445c1c56277&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4bd01507&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFuwJ3NiRrfDXjHH02l5l%252Ffooter-3-footer-bottom.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6ecd2b1-8bd0-492a-b56e-a73745ca94a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86c5f72e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-12-men-fashion#upload-settings-for-footer)

# Home 13 - Winter Sport | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fno7wdQYUYTQw9Z0ITW2M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8c98482-58f2-46f0-8104-3816fbc91e66&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af5d092e&sv=2)

► To setup Footer Home 13 - Winter Sport, you need to add the **Footer 01** section to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F9mbM0AHnKYUW53GGy7a8%252Ffooter-11-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b1202ff-4976-44b5-899c-70aaa82aa0c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b4f210a&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 2. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5TrZeqaIO3PZ351i9WKs%252Ffooter-1-setting-8.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24ac04bb-bbf1-4e9a-96af-dc50509c506b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6aa37d5&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

*   The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFEFZPuDqAHwkciCpLAh3%252Ffooter-1-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D510f35e2-1aec-4beb-93dd-4e8ba664fe4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=892c3872&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FN8LSpp6U2Os3V1USXtDj%252Ffooter-1-setting-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D942496f4-32d7-439f-b66e-6b8acf106f7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=982bf192&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWTqd4vCeg8r2APFaz9mp%252Ffooter-1-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4b426e-83e7-42fd-a3e1-be68fbb23f60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=486960e1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-13-winter-sport#upload-settings-for-footer)

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-13-winter-sport#preset-for-footer-home-13-winter-sport)
     [arrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/ag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi/~/changes/453/footer/new-footer-section-group-layout/layout-01#preset-for-footer-layout-01)

# Product Combo | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F7b4dlcXU5ZMHuhbjT5iJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82259cb6-b5a9-431d-ac9f-60c88da104e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be5ff10f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#id-01-set-up-product-combo)

01 - Set up Product Combo


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#create-a-metafield-for-bundle)

**Create a Metafield for Bundle:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Metafields**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    
3.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FHuHwJSmTE4hJDFobGBBX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfff31152-1965-48c5-850c-3052b2749235&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d0dd83a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#how-to-create-one-more-metafields-to-specify-which-items-will-in-the-product-combo)

How to create one more Metafields to specify which items will in the Product Combo

Repeat the same process we noted above.

*   For the Name: you can enter anything you want.
    

circle-info

The Namespace and Key must be _**"c\_f.product\_combo"**_ for the function to work.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FSSegVCR31fvHibY8vUwe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3b737bb-41a1-4aa9-afc2-994290460757&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9473524a&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FpshMOQaUK5FDFR0yp3Ru%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D12a3e769-e9f8-4272-95cd-06e39b205902&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe130f78&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#id-02-create-product-combo-in-the-database)

02 - Create Product Combo in the database

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products section -> Click "Add Product" button**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FQAiro3s2ln06UBJTv4AR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47c141ea-da43-4811-962b-dd301cc29a5a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c2093285&sv=2)

**2.** Enter the **title** and **description** for Product Combo.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwtU5tYlvHD9UjYfYoeTF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c02ea12-f9f8-4cda-8f61-960fe5ebb4eb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9365a071&sv=2)

**3.** Upload some images about the Product Combo to the **Media Section**.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FM0hyNNAHvwquJowTkxu8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De22d0b7e-edc9-40fc-bfa3-124b70127661&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d04e8c4&sv=2)

**4\.** Scroll down to the **Product Metafields** section, you will see the **2 Metafields** you created a moment ago **"Product Combo" and " Combo Discount Rate"**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FefMTTndZcOEmP9jx9Y5x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2fcb6b97-95d2-496e-8a8b-e519365c4ff5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c18f2d48&sv=2)

**5.** Go to **another Tab**, select some Product you want to add to the **Combo**.

**Tip:** Right click and open the Products on the new tabs.

**6\.** On each Product, Scroll down to the **Search Engine Listing** section and copy its handle, then past it to the **Product Combo Metafield.**

**Note:** Repeat the same process with all the product you want to add to the **Combo.**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FpN0VZdbKIKPLTboaarhI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06ebabf9-420b-4e61-90e3-0cd9059aff0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=518f32a3&sv=2)

> **The handle in Product Combo must be separated with a Comma.**

[PreviousProduct Bundlechevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle)
[NextQuick Order Listchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/quick-order-list)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [01 - Set up Product Combo](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#id-01-set-up-product-combo)
    
*   [Create a Metafield for Bundle:](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#create-a-metafield-for-bundle)
    
*   [How to create one more Metafields to specify which items will in the Product Combo](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#how-to-create-one-more-metafields-to-specify-which-items-will-in-the-product-combo)
    
*   [02 - Create Product Combo in the database](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-combo#id-02-create-product-combo-in-the-database)
    

Copy

    Name: Combo Discount Rate or any name.
    Namespace and key: c_f.combo_discount_rate
    Select content type: Integer

Copy

    Name: Product Combo or any name.
    Namespace and key: c_f.product_combo
    Select content type: Single Line Text

# Home 10 - Jewelry | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FoRhLS6Wq1knu4nfRGrhl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3080eeb2-06fa-41f2-8ed3-79df9ee9459d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17e2853f&sv=2)

[Home 10 - Jewelryarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127103578)

To setup Footer Home 10 - Jewelry, you need to add the **Footer 02** section to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 02** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FL7eI3Kac5LjtPG7VCUJp%252Ffooter-10-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca9ede81-6cf1-441e-8290-54c2dd20aa2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcf34895&sv=2)

In the **Footer 02** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    
    *   The settings are for the block width, title, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
        
    
    ![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FEe1MO7cCkUVgi3LioZpf%252Ffooter-10-newsletter.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92e41d1d-a5ce-4e67-b257-2a4ecb89c71d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=401dbdda&sv=2)
    
    *   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons.
        
    
    ![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FG153wmRgtmGHD0Nc0Adc%252Ffooter-2-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf2ea6c2-99bc-4acc-b154-b05a96a1cd26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86fa57ae&sv=2)
    
    *   The block also allows the border right enabling to separate itself from other block such as text or menu.
        
    
    ![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FxUOPtjLm67FgQwvnQxP4%252Ffooter-2-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32526c37-f6c5-48f1-ab2f-2d0240ed2309&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56fe5204&sv=2)
    
2.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvHQLpfLSzhMz3HFSkXYS%252Ffooter-10-setting-footer-bottom.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68f2d209-1fc4-4280-bf30-b1981be75f18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a3d153c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-10-jewelry#upload-settings-for-footer)

# Home 15 - Automotive 2 | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FkxAQM3jcLZnkbx8OogUs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fba9213-26e7-4339-b474-e654251b5930&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1c47e04&sv=2)

To setup Footer Home 15 - Automotive 2, you need to add the **Newsletter** and **Footer 05** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Newsletter** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 05** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FylA8vZag99NsOce3l1Wf%252Ffooter-6-add-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4ee4d38-3fb5-4c93-ab6f-2f874599ac11&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b27d5a3&sv=2)

► In the **Newsletter** section settings. Add or adjust **Newsletter** block as your need:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FoA9sfQ3C3CyxPVLANYO2%252Ffooter-6-newsletter-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D280a2c7f-fec4-40cc-a587-e101f58a557e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfd4b235&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 05** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.

[Home 11 - Health & Beautyarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127169114)

► To setup Footer Home 11 - Health & Beauty, you need to add the **Footer 01** section to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F9mbM0AHnKYUW53GGy7a8%252Ffooter-11-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b1202ff-4976-44b5-899c-70aaa82aa0c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b4f210a&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 2. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5TrZeqaIO3PZ351i9WKs%252Ffooter-1-setting-8.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24ac04bb-bbf1-4e9a-96af-dc50509c506b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6aa37d5&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

*   The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFEFZPuDqAHwkciCpLAh3%252Ffooter-1-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D510f35e2-1aec-4beb-93dd-4e8ba664fe4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=892c3872&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FN8LSpp6U2Os3V1USXtDj%252Ffooter-1-setting-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D942496f4-32d7-439f-b66e-6b8acf106f7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=982bf192&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWTqd4vCeg8r2APFaz9mp%252Ffooter-1-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4b426e-83e7-42fd-a3e1-be68fbb23f60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=486960e1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-11-health-and-beauty#upload-settings-for-footer)

Upload Settings For Footer


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 11 - Health & Beauty, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-11-health-and-beauty#preset-for-footer-home-11-health-and-beauty)
     [arrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/ag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi/~/changes/453/footer/new-footer-section-group-layout/layout-01#preset-for-footer-layout-01)
    the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRPtqwgG6ABSZWhqME4z6%252Ffooter-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3b1071-06c8-4f29-b2cb-cf36a84c9363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9f9ffab&sv=2)

# Sold In Last Period | Ella Documentation

**Sold in last period** is a feature boosting your sales by making visitors think that the product was purchased by other customers. Then visitors have a belief in your product and decide to buy it.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FqQsj5OMf1ZgttbPCATGK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd19d558d-33b1-4004-bd56-9d50e224238c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9af00791&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Meta**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F60xVUtXNHqpL1XocejWC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7dd4d54-270f-4601-9fa0-db7eaa9f1fde&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1003b310&sv=2)

# Color Comparison | Ella Documentation

**Color Comparison** provides your customers a visual look and comparison between many colors of a product. After that, they can easily make a purchase decision and be satisfied more with the choice.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Ff227ViA0W6j4AyCHdb9E%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f6b7047-141a-4311-9cb1-110a3259b1aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a255a6e&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Perks**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FbW1wPipZm2DKYGzJ9uWg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb9d853b-1a59-4273-b54b-43271b8e7ab4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64758f02&sv=2)

# Dynamic Checkout Button | Ella Documentation

Using the payment methods available on your store, customers see their preferred option, like PayPal or Apple Pay. For more information, see [Dynamic checkout buttonsarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/online-store/dynamic-checkout)
.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** -> Choose **Buy buttons**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F1PQ38WadVGmKFFYiRphs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2f67991-463d-4519-9382-6e4294c8fe15&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34ec31da&sv=2)

# Variant Image Grouped | Ella Documentation

circle-info

Note: This feature only works well on products with a single variant using color swatches.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/variant-image-grouped#below-is-the-step-by-step-instruction-to-set-up-variant-image-grouped)

Below is the step by step instruction to set up Variant image grouped.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/variant-image-grouped#create-a-metafield-for-variants)

**Create a Metafield for** variants**:**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Variants → Add definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FeYuijpruSm0ckyV1f5Nh%252Fmetafield-variant.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0c3a911-23bf-4159-809d-7b491daa41dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50208871&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FfLiMgpOvLx6DS3ZhpQtK%252Fmetafield-variant-define.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10793157-307d-4cd2-9eb1-9a94a5d46b20&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11fee798&sv=2)

3\. Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FaqpHY0rOBLukPcjnvnOF%252Fmetafield-variant-define-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35e4a6d6-c137-40c8-912b-9be4d9b39e32&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=480c5371&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/variant-image-grouped#how-to-insert-content-for-variants-metafields)

How to insert content for Variants Metafields?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  Click on the image -> Click **Add alt text** -> Enter the alt text that you want for the image -> click **Save alt text.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FsxM6c37Sxvho6JI57Lj1%252Fmetafield-variant-product-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8ecde26-b46f-4c44-a5b9-0337a6b1e1a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=957fecaf&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FfEzya2NuaCCFDJZnNhH2%252Fmetafield-variant-product-3c.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5d2f3675-6b04-4d02-8418-b238380c3706&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f8b8ce&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5k5GELU9ndk1WDWp9s0V%252Fmetafield-variant-product-3d.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f5ceee1-a77d-4074-bee4-3bb1e1caab62&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8cc2bd31&sv=2)

1.  At "**Variants**" click on the variant you want.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvUBwm22AHy6wUoPV4NxB%252Fmetafield-variant-product-3k.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16dc7f44-d459-48c1-a1f6-973ac5fbd9e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f62aa190&sv=2)

1.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the alt text of the images you want show for this variant on the **Variant Image Grouped** input.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FewlYEkD59lx57sJjmki8%252Fmetafield-variant-product-3e.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De48cc594-156a-46ab-8d72-b0f41d8c9e39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be00a104&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note**: After each Alt Text, there must be a comma "**,**" and no space between the Alt Texts. **Example**: Gym For Sale Green 1**,**Gym For Sale Green 2

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/variant-image-grouped#set-up-variant-image-grouped)

**Set up** Variant Image Grouped


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Variant picker.**
    
5.  Choose **Enable variant image grouped** to enable Variant Image Grouped function.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FEgZAtEemQaTviro2kxMS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7abd2e99-03be-4511-afc3-e129ecb7ef38&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6dadde56&sv=2)

Here is the result:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5kftEB5Z7btkzJytSNvC%252Fmetafield-variant-product-3h.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88e71e4f-6eb4-48ed-a9fe-d23e74b274f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a5df1d4&sv=2)

circle-info

If you want to have this feature on **Quickview**, please go to **Theme settings -> Quickview** -> **Enable variant image grouped**.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FUkOB4WjMoI7ubT9QkzWL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D776f9483-d694-4137-9322-86c88afc73c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=683e91f4&sv=2)

[PreviousList Tagschevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/list-tags)
[NextProduct Bundlechevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle)

Last updated 9 months ago

*   [Below is the step by step instruction to set up Variant image grouped.](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/variant-image-grouped#below-is-the-step-by-step-instruction-to-set-up-variant-image-grouped)

    Name: Variant Image Grouped or any name.
    Namespace and key: custom.variant_image_group
    Select content type: Multi-line text

# Sticky Add To Cart | Ella Documentation

**Sticky Add To Cart** helps customers make a purchase as easy as possible. An impossible-to-miss Add to cart popup is always visible on the product detailed page and urges customers to checkout.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FcyyIGaGOkUUFTTE8YU6y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51972ab2-91c4-44f9-8216-f110dd00787e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5c2a3d0&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  Click on the **Product information** section -> scroll down to **STICKY ADD TO CART.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FplGdBH22QT4iie9LoNGa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37eb8ba5-8365-4fda-adf0-a2165d46abfb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=645f9550&sv=2)

# Custom Information | Ella Documentation

**Custom Information** shows us features such as delivery date, technical specification, shipping or other crucial notes of the product.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Faf5rPuTCgFhV4ZnVbfWd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De91824b2-f26c-4f2b-851a-c1aa7b001e2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=faa3798a&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product Information ->** Click **Add block** -> Choose **Custom information**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOchb69gbFwlsPMJxLmLg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a22a91c-60d5-47e2-9ec6-b425dbeacf43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6541bfc9&sv=2)

[NextHow To Set Up Product Description For Each Variant?chevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-description-for-each-variant)

# Customers Viewing | Ella Documentation

**Customers Viewing** is a feature boosting your sales by making visitors think that the product was viewed by other customers. Then visitors have a belief in your product and decide to buy it.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F38aA2NDAuZHxm5np6w3o%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4dcacbf4-63d0-424b-bd23-faa6d1496a9b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15a9cd49&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product Information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Customers viewing**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FlKs5EEQeJnHfWZtplBQv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a7e6205-94d0-4c06-9620-9c870fff2e2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15b98a54&sv=2)

# Collection header | Ella Documentation

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#section-settings)

Section settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#general)

General

Setting

Description

Section layout

Select the layout for the section, there are 3 options: **Style 1 Style 2 Style 3**

Show breadcrumb

Enable to show the breadcrumb.

Breadcrumb alignment

Align the breadcrumb to either the center, left, or right.

Color - Background - Background gradient

Set the text color and background for the breadcrumb on the desktop.

Mobile color - Background color on mobile - Background gradient on mobile

Set the text color and background for the breadcrumb on the mobile.

Show page title

Enable to show the page title.

Page title alignment

Align the page title to either the center, left, or right.

Section width

Select the layout width of the whole section. The options are: **Default (same as the body width) Width (1170px) Width (1770px) Full width (100% of the viewport width)**

Padding for 'full width' option on desktop

Determine the left and right spacing of the full width layout.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#section-top-padding)

Section top padding

Settings

Meaning

Desktop

Determines the height of the top inner space of the section on the desktop device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Tablet

Determines the height of the top inner space of the section on the tablet device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Mobile

Determines the height of the top inner space of the section on the mobile device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#section-bottom-padding)

Section bottom padding

Settings

Meaning

Desktop

Determines the height of the bottom inner space of the section on the desktop device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Tablet

Determines the height of the bottom inner space of the section on the tablet device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Mobile

Determines the height of the bottom inner space of the section on the mobile device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#block-settings)

Block settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#block-collection-image)

\[BLOCK\] Collection image

_To change collection descriptions or collection images,_ [_edit your collections._arrow-up-right](https://admin.shopify.com/store/hoanghiepsoftware/collections)

Settings

Meaning

Show parallax banner

Enable to apply parallax layout for banner.

Show background overlay

Enable to apply background overlay for banner.

Type

Select the style for the banner, there are 2 options: **Custom Full width**

Upload image

Select the image and apply it to all collections.

Upload image for mobile

Select the image and apply it to all collections on mobile.

Background overlay color

Set background overlay color for banner.

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#there-are-2-ways-to-setup-banner)

**There are 2 ways to setup banner:**

1.  Upload one image for all collections: You can upload it right in the theme editor. Please choose **Collection Image** as below:
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FkGeDlNEdJfghSxZdkSCf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1617f8b-7704-4d0b-b0dc-7f65b8c18a8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c6a7d4a&sv=2)

2\. Upload different image for different collections: **don't upload an image in the theme editor of Collection Image**. Go to **Collection Admin** -> Upload an image at here:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FqMjhCQixWW5a6rCm4qQz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b3f85b9-e70f-4f26-99f3-a13b31fbf1f2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a754c886&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/collection-header#block-collection-description)

\[BLOCK\] Collection description

Settings

Meaning

**Description**

Show collection description

Enable to show collection description.

Show 'read more'/'read less'

Enable to show 'read more'/'read less' button for collection description.

Position

Select the display position of the collection description. There are 2 options: **Relative**

**Absolute**

Content alignment

The alignment of the collection description vertically within the banner. _Note: Only applies for 'position: absolute'._

Alignment

The alignment of the collection description horizontally within the banner.

Page content max width

Set the maximum width of the collection description. Unit %.

Text color - Background - Background gradient

Set the text color and background color for collection description.

**Sub-collection**

Show sub-collection

Enable to show sub-collection.

Sub-collection layout

Select the layout for sub-collection.

Sub collection max height

Determine max height for sub-collection. _Note: Use for grid layout._

Position

Select the position for sub-collection. There are 2 options: **Relative**

**Absolute**

Show

Select to limit the display of sub-collection items. There are 2 options: **All sub-collections** (show all items) **Some sub-collections** (show only 5 items)

Background - Background gradient

Set the background/gradient for sub-collection.

Top padding

Determine the spacing top of the sub-collection.

Bottom padding

Determine the spacing bottom of the sub-collection.

Title

Enter the title for the sub-collection.

Color

Set the color for the title.

Font size

Set the font size for the title.

Font weight

Set the font weight for the title.

Text style

Set the text transform for the title.

Show sub-collection image

Enable to show sub-collection image.

Item top padding

Determine the spacing top of each item.

Item bottom padding

Determine the spacing bottom of each item.

Grid gap

Determine the spacing between 2 items.

Color - Background - Background gradient - Border color - Hover color - Background hover color - Background hover gradient - Border hover color

Set the text color, background, and border color for both the normal and hover states of the item.

Section top padding

Determine the spacing top of the sub-collection section.

# Delivery Time | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F6dUG83CM3BtGzmG562KX%252Fdelivery_time.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41e8c661-0efa-4d5c-9ce7-3c539e6b7841&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f803424e&sv=2)

**Delivery Time** helps customers know the estimated delivery time from the moment they place an order through the settings on your store.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Delivery time**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FcNYO50qmHYHHWkGf1S1l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D996dbd07-c881-4c67-ac85-c984f23d648a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fafe00fb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/delivery-time#block-settings)

Block settings

Settings

Meaning

Icon

Enter the SVG icon

Icon size

Determine icon size.

Text/Icon color

Apply a color for the text and icon.

Delivery text

Add the text you want to display on Delivery Time. The values: **hour**, **date\_start**, and **date\_end** must be placed in \[…\]; otherwise, the exact time cannot be displayed. _Example: 'Order within the next \[hour\] to receive it. Estimated delivery is between \[date\_start\] and \[date\_end\]' or 'Order in the next \[hour\] to get this to you between \[date\_start\] and \[date\_end\]' or 'Order in the next \[hour\] to get it by \[date\_end\]' or 'Order in the next \[hour\] to get it soon'_

Text font size

Specify the font size of the text.

Start date from current date

Set **Delivery Start Date**: **2 days**; **today** is **Thursday, May 23**, and **Exclude Days** **SAT, SUN** (You have excluded Saturday, May 25, and Sunday, May 26).

End date from current date

Set **Delivery End Date**: **6 days**; **today** is **Thursday, May 23,** and **Exclude Days** **SAT, SUN** => **Wednesday, May 29.**

Exclude days from

Add the day in a week that you wanna exclude. There are 2 options: **Only delivery Shipping + Delivery**

Date format

Select a format you would like to use.

Cut-off

Set the time within the day when you want to cut off delivery here. _Note: Number only (24 hours format - 16:00:00 means 4PM)_

'Hours' text - 'Minutes' text

This option allows you can customize the text of the Text hours/ minutes. **Example**: Instead of using "**hours**/**minutes**," you can set it as "**h**/**mins**". Or you can set it to be suitable for your country's language.

Top padding

Determine the spacing of the block from top.

Bottom padding

Determine the spacing of the block from bottom.

# Filter | Ella Documentation

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Apps**.
    
2.  Type to find "**Search & Discovery**" app of Shopify
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FDqfl1FQVadb6kW4A3Hdk%252Ffilter_setup_1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a3a4105-f5c0-4a03-a797-9e08cb3625c3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c032c3ae&sv=2)

**OR** go to **Navigation -> Add App** like the below image:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FMPCOdrxNb5PeM6Ma67mV%252Ffilter_setup_2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e8d34c4-5b18-40c8-a291-f219c13a45c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f71e7cb&sv=2)

1.  Open **App** -> Click **Filters.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FQx4edOTiIw1mXcp8p4nL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc75d6311-cc1c-4571-98d3-7881d29a5df1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=550bc932&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Filter.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvfDil6fHD20fPooucr88%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f2811e0-b8f4-4a75-8295-148df7b4beec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b3f13ef&sv=2)

1.  Choose option filter you want to set up.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFEFNgAJuJU7CMDj1DA1L%252Ffilter_setup_5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bfe1d60-a248-4174-8624-d0a9054a7cb9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b7658e1&sv=2)

circle-info

If your product collection contains **over 5000 products**, then filters are hidden. For more information, see [Add storefront filteringarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/online-store/themes/customizing-themes/storefront-filters)
.

circle-info

If you used storefront filters prior to **August 16, 2022**, the settings to manage your saved filters moved to the Shopify Search & Discovery app. - The app has been preinstalled to your admin, so you can continue to edit your filters.

\- The app will not impact your store’s performance.

\=> If you want to get more information, [please visit the linkarrow-up-right](https://shopify.pxf.io/kj74K3)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection/filter#set-up-filter-options-in-theme-editor)

S**et up filter options in Theme Editor**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Collection** from the dropdown window. Scroll to **Filter** at **Main Collection ->** click the **Show Product Filtering?** checkbox to enable the filter.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFUaK4HMlebzZMqdYCRrM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25d7fbd7-ea2d-4078-a329-39c3272d3a2e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16badd1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection/filter#custom-style-for-filter-option)

Custom style for Filter option


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Ella offers 3 styles for Filter option: **Checkbox**, **Swatch** or **Rectangle**. If you would like to use **Swatch** or **Rectangle** style, please follow instructions below.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store ->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Collection** from the dropdown window. After that, scroll to **Filter** at **Main Collection**
    
4.  Enter Filter Option Name for Swatch style in **Swatch Style For Filter** text box (or enter Filter Option Name for **Rectangle** **Type for Filter**).
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fqla0AGgwJkBZVhEV4dXD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11767366-7023-455f-8e06-a094ab7fceef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff335eef&sv=2)

circle-info

The default theme uses Color Board from the [w3schools websitearrow-up-right](https://www.w3schools.com/colors/colors_names.asp)
 for the Color variant option. If the color name doesn't exist on the [w3schools websitearrow-up-right](https://www.w3schools.com/colors/colors_names.asp)
, it will not display on your site.

circle-info

With Color swatch filter option, if your products have custom color/special color, please choose **Swatch Type** as **Basic Color (Use Color name or Image With PNG Format)**.

After that, please upload an image with the same name as the variant color name (Go to Settings → Files -> Upload Files).

Your image must be in **PNG** format

**Naming convention**: Lower cap and use a hyphen "-" to replace white space if your color image name has the white space.

For example: your special color will have this name: "Holo Rainbow", you will upload the png image is: holo-rainbow.png

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection/filter#tag-filter)

Tag Filter


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up Filter By Tag.

**Step 1**: Go go **Customize** theme -> Choose **Collection** from the dropdown window. At **Main Collection**, click **Add block** -> Choose "**\[Sidebar\]** **Filter**"

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FY5BqCdfEb3MtnPMruWHU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77738d56-2fd9-43cd-9d50-d6cac92e759f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cc0c16b&sv=2)

**Step 2:** Enter heading and list tags you want to filter.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F8FD0seV12YXVSJwKP0ct%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca2a8d47-e940-47ce-81df-4e4bddbb8ee8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=43b2043f&sv=2)

circle-info

*   Maximum for showing **50 blocks per section**.
    
*   Separate by a **comma**. i.e: red**,**blue**,**yellow.
    
*   **Required Condition:** The tag you add in Editor and the tag you add to your products must be the same. Take note for **Lowercase and Uppercase**. If they are different, they will not show.
    

Step 3: Go to Navigation -> Open App -> Choose Filter -> Enable option **More filters**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FCR3wpNsgPavApeby2ye6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd092e9a-ea2b-4786-85b1-23a88786dd11&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95495fb6&sv=2)

> **Pro Tip:** If you don't want to show **Tags** in **Filter Sidebar**, you can apply **Hidden Tag Filter** in **Main Collection** Setting.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fh26DrBeWrt9xf8Lm1zbW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22d3bc15-8d46-4728-bc0b-e756223594c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6859141&sv=2)

[PreviousMain collectionchevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection)
[NextDemo & Settings Datachevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/demo-and-settings-data)

# List Tags | Ella Documentation

**List tags** will display all the tags of the product within the Products Setting in the Shopify admin.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FNRK1wagZ0CPRi2jiUIwy%252Fpositive-vibes-bundle-on-the-product-card-38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadc857e3-61ea-4703-aef6-cd84889d57b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f01b6f7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/list-tags#below-is-the-step-by-step-instruction-to-set-up-list-tags)

Below is the step by step instruction to set up List Tags.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Tags list**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FILmTyjwVoZgLHIuLGLtV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D730fd948-2a82-4290-9de1-87eea0e73620&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28a63bda&sv=2)

# Description | Ella Documentation

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Description**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FKBKOetSaPW1wsDKtYqsx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D529fa32d-80ce-4406-be57-8b630136cdd2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89bee92f&sv=2)

circle-info

Ella offers you to show **Description** by Metafields. If a product have no short description in metafield, it will show a brief product summary (the first 50 characters of the description).

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/description#setup-short-description-by-metafields)

Setup Short Description by Metafields?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/description#how-to-add-new-metafields)

**How to add new Metafields?**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPTqNndRguDzb15QPCqT0%252Fmeta-field.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904657ee-9381-4d21-a258-56b1c8d7c2bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56c7e2e9&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F6kCGWPIU2szu8E4bBeyi%252Fshort-description-1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9752229b-1cc3-4e9e-a38c-fac6513f6306&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33a378cf&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/description#how-to-insert-content-for-product-metafields)

How to insert content for Product Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields**, please insert content for "**Short Description**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FKyGTQA0DEzDPXYiSGYCq%252Fshort-description-2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f4c6985-2e03-4b34-bcd1-9e06961088cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=98ac3181&sv=2)

circle-info

You can use Bulk Editor to edit multiple products.

[NextDelivery Timechevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/delivery-time)

# Main collection | Ella Documentation

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#section-settings)

Section settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#general)

General

Setting

Description

Section width

Select the layout width of the whole section. The options are: **Default (same as the body width) Width (1170px) Width (1770px) Full width (100% of the viewport width)**

Padding for 'full width' option on desktop

Determine the left and right spacing of the full width layout.

Background color - Background color

Set the background/gradient for the section.

Setting

Description

Collapsible block style

Turn the blocks in sidebar to be collapsible.

Enable sticky sidebar

Fix the position of the sidebar when scrolling until the end of the collection content.

Layout

Determine how collapsible blocks are presented: **Style 1** (The collapsible blocks appear with carets) **Style 2** (The collapsible blocks appear with minus and plus icons)

Collapsible

Select the collapse state of the collapsible blocks when the page loads.

Type

Select how the sidebar is presented. There are 2 options: **Vertical** (the sidebar will lie on the left or the right of the page) **Horizontal** ( the sidebar will lie on the beginning of the page)

Position

Select the position of the side to be either to the Left or Right.

**Block heading**

Font family

Select the font family for the heading of the sidebar.

Font size

Determine the font size of the heading of the sidebar.

Font weight

Select the font weight of the heading of the sidebar

Text style

Select the text transform for the heading of the sidebar

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#filter)

Filter

Setting

Description

Show product filtering

Enable to show product filtering on the sidebar.

Swatch style for filter

Input filter name to show swatch style.

Swatch type

Select the type for the swatch. There are 2 options:

**Basic color** (use color name) **Advanced color** (use image with PNG format)

Swatch layout

Select the layout for the swatch. There are 3 options: **Color swatch Color swatch with name Color swatch with name and count**

Rectangle style for filter

Input filter name to show rectangle style

Filter display

Select how to display filters. There are 2 options:

**Scrolling Show more button**

Maximum items per filter

Determine the maximum number of items displayed when the page loads. _Note: used for filter display: show more button._

Filter label for all tags

When using a name other than the label 'more filters,' please enter the label name according to the name you've set in this setting.

Apply hidden tag filter

Enter the product tags that you don't want to display in filter by tag. _Note: Separate by a comma, i.e 'red,blue,yellow'._

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#toolbar)

Toolbar

Setting

Description

Show toolbar

Enable to show the toolbar.

Show sorting

Enable to show the sorting.

Show 'items per page'

Enable to show the 'items per page'.

Show 'view as'

Enable to show the 'view as'.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#product)

Product

Setting

Description

Maximum products per page

Determine the maximum number of products displayed on 1 page.

Layout

Select layout when displaying product items.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#pagination)

Pagination

Setting

Description

Pagination

Select the pagination function. There are 3 options: **Pagination Show more button Infinite scroll**

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#product-banner-in-collection)

Product banner in collection

_Use for layout 'collections banner advertisement'_

Setting

Description

Enable banner

Enable to show the banners for layout 'collections banner advertisement'.

Enable banner #1/#2/#3

Enable to show the banner #1/#2/#3

Banner position #1/#2/#3

Enter the position/order of the item you want to display the banner #1/#2/#3.

Image 1/2/3

Select the image for the banner 1/2/3.

Link 1/2/3

Enter the link for the banner 1/2/3.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#grid)

Grid

Setting

Description

Space between vertical

Determine the vertical distance between two items on the desktop.

Space between vertical mobile

Determine the vertical distance between two items on the mobile.

Space between horizontal

Determine the horizontal distance between two items on the desktop.

Space between horizontal mobile

Determine the horizontal distance between two items on the mobile.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#top-padding)

Top padding

Settings

Meaning

Desktop

Determines the height of the top inner space of the section on the desktop device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Tablet

Determines the height of the top inner space of the section on the tablet device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Mobile

Determines the height of the top inner space of the section on the mobile device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/collections-page/collection-section/main-collection#bottom-padding)

Bottom padding

Settings

Meaning

Desktop

Determines the height of the bottom inner space of the section on the desktop device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Tablet

Determines the height of the bottom inner space of the section on the tablet device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).

Mobile

Determines the height of the bottom inner space of the section on the mobile device. Can be from 0px to 100px, increasing arithmetically of 5px (pixel).
