# Product Bundle | Ella Documentation

**Product bundle** helps customers add additional products besides the main product. They will get a discount when adding to cart all products in the bundle. This is also a way to boost your sale.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FGwxQ9AHVmtPd1HpYuous%252F134.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4dab0e-75cd-4526-bebc-d373b2b394f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c68480f5&sv=2)

Instruction video

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#id-01-set-up-product-bundle)

01 - Set up Product Bundle


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#create-a-metafield-for-bundle)

**Create a Metafield for Bundle:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPTqNndRguDzb15QPCqT0%252Fmeta-field.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904657ee-9381-4d21-a258-56b1c8d7c2bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56c7e2e9&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FrDwofFUfEf5z7OBFAEWZ%252Fbundle-1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D353945b9-0b21-45f2-8c43-63eba8d85a66&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62abb01b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#how-to-insert-content-for-product-metafields)

How to insert content for Product Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the handle of sub products for "**Grouped Sub Product**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FJ3nWnlGECx9ARMqM4m56%252Fbundle-2.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09af5e62-18c1-4fc6-8826-2680c4fe6db2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=999c9e1b&sv=2)

circle-info

To get handle of sub products, please go to Admin -> Products -> choose the product you want to add in bundle -> Scroll down at the bottom to see **Search engine listing preview** -> click **Edit website SEO** -> copy **Product handle**. [Learn morearrow-up-right](https://shopify.dev/api/liquid/basics/handle)
.

circle-info

You can use Bulk Editor to edit multiple products.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#id-02-set-up-discount-rate-for-product-bundle)

02 - Set up Discount Rate For Product Bundle


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#create-a-collection-with-a-group-of-products)

Create A Collection with a group of products:

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> Collections**.
    
2.  Create a collection which _**contains all of products in the bundle you created**_**.** The name of this collection will be: **BUNDLE-xxxxxxxxx** (with **x** will be _**product ID of main product in bundle**_).
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fe4EoTiIhCjx97WFEpG6F%252Fbundle-2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab4ab76f-bdd0-4316-baf3-1cce89969c19&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5eb0ae94&sv=2)

Create a collection which contains all of products in the bundle you created

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FoJQBZb7c53ZXecn47k7M%252Fbundle-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9369df9e-d4a2-4e46-9e78-2db350d24b4a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c99c634e&sv=2)

Product ID of main product in bundle

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#create-a-discount-for-bundle)

Create A Discount for Bundle

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Discounts. ->** Click **Create discount**.
    
2.  Create a discount for the bundle collection you just created. The name of this discount will be: **FBT-BUNDLE-xxxxxxxxx** (with **x** will be _**product ID of main product in bundle**_).
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FKZ9CFBlqpfKK8pUEjji2%252Fbundle-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd57b9e6-7c05-4697-9ced-a2da9dbdbbf0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59c40f96&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FeT30U9HRR6eiaR2VacO6%252Fbundle-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad7dd0f8-5214-4b81-8260-415645935b6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1d95722&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#how-to-add-a-new-metafields)

**How to add a new Metafields?**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPTqNndRguDzb15QPCqT0%252Fmeta-field.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904657ee-9381-4d21-a258-56b1c8d7c2bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56c7e2e9&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F4fDpS0EGGNCvns1WjaDl%252Fbundle-3.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dedbf3a77-aac1-49c7-a5c4-a17ad2988e27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=214f1f29&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#how-to-insert-content-for-product-metafields-1)

How to insert content for Product Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields** area, please enter discount value which you just created for "**Bundle Discount Rate**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FzMbrtZYPyXFof1XbOZlC%252Fbundle-4.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd7a7811-8b2e-4ecd-89f3-25b7c8ec0f1e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=acd095d8&sv=2)

circle-info

You can use Bulk Editor to edit multiple products.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-bundle#customize-product-bundle)

Customize Product Bundle


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Products** from the dropdown window.
    
4.  Click **Product information ->** scroll down to **Product bundle**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FuRjJU4AaYdObhQ6DGEt8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb11fb06-7578-42d6-ab97-06ede42be08a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56d8b4f7&sv=2)

# How To Set Up Product Description For Each Variant? | Ella Documentation

The [Add product variant metafieldarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/shopify-flow/reference/actions/update-product-variant-metafield)
 action adds a metafield to the product variant that triggers the workflow, or updates an existing metafield on that product variant.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-description-for-each-variant#how-to-add-new-variant-metafields)

**How to add new Variant Metafields?**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Variants → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FB2VEWQ5cZrFKdsbPegCG%252FScreenshot_1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56ee50c3-ac41-4aaa-a0b9-f96c8d818bb6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=634221f1&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwiQVHk7sGdoA4vECP6mN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1467e495-4a13-46c4-9cfd-bea63e925e1f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4af6474f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-description-for-each-variant#how-to-insert-content-for-variant-metafields)

How to insert content for Variant Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  Choose variant to edit.
    
4.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the content for "**Variant Description**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FovFKtqklIWtwhxRFz6pg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20e9a7d9-cab2-4719-ad67-791c5758b7d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=522b5c50&sv=2)

# Home 37 - Craft Beer | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fc80oyP7vZ1d8zrRndhsc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D923e30bf-e39a-4073-a157-68f8e6275329&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6635d23e&sv=2)

► To set up the footer for **Home 37 - Craft Beer**, you need to add the **Footer 01** section to the **Footer Group**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **Footer Group ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F9U2fVB6YCbPaMyYo52S4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83ff3adf-d09b-481a-b67b-340b3829b24d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a0ad24d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-37-craft-beer#upload-settings-for-footer)

Upload Settings For Footer


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 37 - Craft Beer please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to download](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-37-craft-beer#preset-for-home-35-dietary-supplement)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FJlN5CXzwwf6pdZon1ueR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26e5ead7-5b90-46da-a930-de1852565f18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10a6a287&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-37-craft-beer#preset-for-home-37-craft-beer)

# Home 18 - Shoes | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fj55CK0FVFa5KQ4m3LGiB%252Ffooter-18.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa257dab-1c7b-4ce7-8740-3f091c7c07b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48f8c58a&sv=2)

[Home 18 - Shoesarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123190444122)

► To setup Footer Home 18 - Shoes, you need to add the **Footer 01** section to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOuLaXiaFR8xfbRLeMtu3%252Ffooter-18-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79a6c036-3284-432f-bbe9-bc31156b7646&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e8c3989&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 2. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5TrZeqaIO3PZ351i9WKs%252Ffooter-1-setting-8.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24ac04bb-bbf1-4e9a-96af-dc50509c506b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6aa37d5&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

*   The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFEFZPuDqAHwkciCpLAh3%252Ffooter-1-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D510f35e2-1aec-4beb-93dd-4e8ba664fe4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=892c3872&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FN8LSpp6U2Os3V1USXtDj%252Ffooter-1-setting-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D942496f4-32d7-439f-b66e-6b8acf106f7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=982bf192&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWTqd4vCeg8r2APFaz9mp%252Ffooter-1-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4b426e-83e7-42fd-a3e1-be68fbb23f60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=486960e1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-18-shoes#upload-settings-for-footer)

# Home 16 - Games | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F7HhAtTNa6WNgE85ICAj9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce6893d6-0b84-4ea9-bc47-bd7ba9ab54dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d1bc71f&sv=2)

[Home 16 - Gamesarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123127365722)

► To setup Footer Home 16 - Games, you need to add the **Policies Block** and **Footer 06** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Policies Block** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 06** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FcXoem3w6lJ0r9M6Tco8F%252Ffooter-16-add-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96353e7b-e463-42a0-b425-aba9061cb831&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fdbf23d&sv=2)

► In the **Policies Block** section settings. Add or adjust **Text** blocks as your need:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FJL0VHWRueUKhh3wijq1w%252Ffooter-16-policies.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db74a729e-45b6-4405-8b69-a03065389ac9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab34f000&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 06** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 1. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FLuZvc8RXRhEFmlPqa38j%252Ffooter-16-text.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b698ea1-a4cf-4c96-b276-b40b1b04f0a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99245a94&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fu6cp5Xs8oadxEK2zaZA2%252Ffooter-16-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D330f0174-d45c-44e3-bdc3-e4c6b4c95319&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e1d9a92&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1. The block will always be at the bottom of the footer 06 section. The settings are for the block width, title, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FKgOuZmk7uCkyC2e74Oga%252Ffooter-16-newsellter-1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D102b6953-9a0d-4ea9-9e37-ec6f3ec7abc4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4803254c&sv=2)

1.  **Show Social Media Icons** block: Limit 1. The block will be at the same row as the Newsletter block on Desktop. On mobile, they will be put on stack of each other to save space.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FmyROYilrWxZ4yIJpXbhQ%252Ffooter-16-social.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bea36e1-3013-4ad1-b55f-76a3e42d1f47&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b75b504&sv=2)

*   **Footer** **Bottom**: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F657b54KV6Kc3asLSMka0%252Ffooter-16-bottom.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cdc85ee-1b88-45ce-956e-09be6af8f1d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47397e69&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F7wDg7SKo4RVL3EDssttE%252Ffooter-16-payment.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74acfd66-034f-4243-b45b-f1d991ae32b1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16d58ed5&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-16-games#upload-settings-for-footer)

Upload Settings For Footer


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 16 - Games, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-16-games#preset-for-footer-home-16-games)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRPtqwgG6ABSZWhqME4z6%252Ffooter-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3b1071-06c8-4f29-b2cb-cf36a84c9363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9f9ffab&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-16-games#preset-for-footer-home-16-games)

# Product Tabs | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F1pf5H5M5zV4nNX2Mrerh%252F135.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec133f37-233a-408e-b8f0-84b20df92722&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1038ce&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FL8LMUXEhnUaV06LTyOXI%252F136.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07a2d062-0370-421e-acdc-09987494dac4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a3a70&sv=2)

circle-info

*   Ella offers you to show 3 different product tab types: Description tab, Review tab and Custom tabs.
    
*   The Custom tabs content can be the same for all products or different for each product.
    
*   You can create multiple different product tabs for your product page.
    

*   Go to **Customize** -> Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FEIMR8oCuBJBIA5oa7esd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De56b9f2c-2ff9-4e2d-9041-d40195ce71de&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d96f0fae&sv=2)

*   Click **Add block** from **Product Information** \-> Choose **Custom tab.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FzO4BaW1OFqdwz9DDmcyK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df728ab86-652a-4fa7-aa2a-f2815b6aa90a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aa82c2ff&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#id-01.-to-show-the-same-tab-content-for-all-products-please-choose-all-products-.-then-enter-the-conten)

**01\. To show the same tab content for all products**, please choose "**All products"**. Then enter the content in the "**Content"** text box. You can use your own html code to style your tab content as you want.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FgXTct6mvSt0PkaS2gLj7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a17c3ab-17a3-4b64-9e83-aa0a764f0431&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79b03d06&sv=2)

**02\. To show the different tab content for each product**, please choose **"Specific products using metafield"**, no need to enter the content in the **"Content"** text box.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F43yvLGwxtB4SBr9d1V58%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da49804ca-70dc-44c4-b711-58226210cdf2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=189f6a25&sv=2)

**Then, Please follow the instructions below to set up the different tab contents.**

**There are 2 ways to set up different contents: by** [**Metafield**](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#setup-custom-tabs-by-metafields)
 **and by** [**Bulk Editor**](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#setup-custom-tabs-by-bulk-editor)
**.**

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#setup-custom-tabs-by-metafields)

**S**etup Custom Tabs by **Metafields**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#step-1-add-a-new-metafields-for-the-tab-you-want-to-create)

**Step 1 - Add a new Metafields for the Tab you want to create**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPTqNndRguDzb15QPCqT0%252Fmeta-field.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904657ee-9381-4d21-a258-56b1c8d7c2bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56c7e2e9&sv=2)

1.  Please enter a **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

> **Name**: Use the name of tab you want
> 
> **Namespace and key**: **c\_f.**XXX
> 
> **Select content type**: Text -> Multi-line Text
> 
> *   (With **c\_f.** is a code you **MUST** use correctly and XXX is the name of tab you want, no white space or if you want to have space, you will use "_" to replace the white space. Example:_ _c\_f.customtab_ _or_ _c\_f.custom\_tab__)_
>     
> *   Remember the key after **c\_**_**f.**_ _to paste it in theme editor of_ _**Step 2.**_ _Example._ _If your Namespace and key is c\_f.customtab so_ _**the key you need to remember is**_ _**customtab**_
>     

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fjiu9Myg8d2Frz7NvzXwD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D943aa4ed-4f52-4abc-bd37-1da5112f3d76&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bc6a53&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#step-2-fill-product-tab-metafield-key)

Step 2: Fill Product Tab Metafield 'Key'

1.  Come back to **Editor of Product Page** -> **Custom Tab** \-> scroll down to the bottom -> **Product Tab Metafield 'Key'.**
    
2.  At **"Product Custom Source",** select **From Entering Metafield Key.**
    
3.  At the **Product Tab Metafield 'Key'** box, fill the key from [**Step 1**](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#step-1-add-a-new-metafields-for-the-tab-you-want-to-create)
     above. Example as above is **customtab**.
    
4.  Save.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FG7GgBYdyWNOieYjTQztI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46787897-81f4-43d9-89ce-cfb52f8afc8c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eae7d084&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-tabs#step-3-insert-the-tab-content-for-each-product-in-the-product-metafields)

Step 3: Insert the tab content for each product in the Product Metafields:

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In **Metafields** area at the bottom, please enter the content in the "**Custom Tab**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F64OYbuFUXnTV6K1mUzgQ%252FScreenshot_16.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c6e2af6-7f54-470a-b846-eb2604a91b74&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56344c42&sv=2)

circle-info

You can use HTML Formatting for Custom Tab content.

Instruction Video for How to set up product tabs with Metafields

[PreviousProduct Mediachevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-media)
[NextProduct Variantchevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/product-variant)

# Positive Vibes Bundle | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtcpxvWEOBetJSSRJ0ZHb%252Fpositive-vibes-bundle-on-the-product-card-17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b804409-587c-4272-8d94-d0a75726fae6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38af47d7&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fn6zAL5Vtt3SoeaORDkMk%252Fpositive-vibes-bundle-on-the-product-card-23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f0ebcfb-62f7-466a-af2c-4083da2435ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67ad5dc2&sv=2)

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** **\->** **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.
    
4.  From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Positive vibes bundle**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FkALfEVOdgj1f182xdzAh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c458136-baa6-4343-a6d3-7c1299165ed9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f924100a&sv=2)

You can use **Metafields** to show "**Positive Vibes Bundle**" by each product.

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/positive-vibes-bundle#how-to-add-new-metafields)

**How to add new Metafields?**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom Data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    
3.  Please enter correct **Name** as we noted below.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FBPkhFtqENIQ9LUA5qfZY%252Fpositive-vibes-bundle-on-the-product-card-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19bbd0a1-a169-431b-af6d-2d9ab3cc5ec6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4f117dd&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FyoLJZiIydFIb8c4eqdqh%252Fpositive-vibes-bundle-on-the-product-card-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D547e1209-9017-4e66-bff1-3e0b0ef8f3d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=113357af&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/positive-vibes-bundle#positive-vibes-over-people)

\- Positive vibes over people

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FyhXwpvF5fGRUyHsFf68r%252Fpositive-vibes-bundle-on-the-product-card-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a1fe83d-0500-49a9-b100-c12f2001b08a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe76307a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/positive-vibes-bundle#how-to-insert-content-for-product-metafields)

How to insert content for Product Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the text that for "**Positive vibes new arrivals**", "**Positive vibes people purchased**", "**Positive vibes sold in the last**" and "**Positive vibes over people**" field.

# Home 20 - Furniture | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FGQ9WkIo4n20Gzyi4cmzK%252Ffooter-20.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De31b7d70-3a3d-40a8-8d8d-16e527f72295&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eaef546a&sv=2)

[Home 20 - Furniturearrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=123360804915)

► To setup Footer Home 20 - Furniture, you need to add the **Policies Block** and **Footer 01** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FwPQTscnFXfrCkhZkGmEr%252Ffooter-20-setting.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3dce528-47e5-4c3b-a3cf-61be4746e7a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e65424e&sv=2)

► In the **Policies Block** section settings. Add or adjust **Text** blocks as your need:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fmu126OaB64v4M38CTA8I%252Ffooter-20-setting-1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fa759f7-4abc-4ba6-9670-995692f29a9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=774aba73&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 2. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F5TrZeqaIO3PZ351i9WKs%252Ffooter-1-setting-8.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24ac04bb-bbf1-4e9a-96af-dc50509c506b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6aa37d5&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtRhAnaZ7wdmieczD8xWW%252Ffooter-1-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da78a6ce3-41b8-466d-b4a1-f55b5edcc5f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edda28b6&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

*   The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFEFZPuDqAHwkciCpLAh3%252Ffooter-1-setting-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D510f35e2-1aec-4beb-93dd-4e8ba664fe4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=892c3872&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FN8LSpp6U2Os3V1USXtDj%252Ffooter-1-setting-4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D942496f4-32d7-439f-b66e-6b8acf106f7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=982bf192&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWTqd4vCeg8r2APFaz9mp%252Ffooter-1-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4b426e-83e7-42fd-a3e1-be68fbb23f60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=486960e1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-20-furniture#upload-settings-for-footer)

Upload Settings For Footer


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 20 - Furniture, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-20-furniture#preset-for-footer-home-20-furniture)
     [arrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/ag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi/~/changes/453/footer/new-footer-section-group-layout/layout-01#preset-for-footer-layout-01)
    the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRPtqwgG6ABSZWhqME4z6%252Ffooter-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3b1071-06c8-4f29-b2cb-cf36a84c9363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9f9ffab&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-20-furniture#preset-for-footer-home-20-furniture)

Preset for **Footer** Home 20 - Furniture

# Home 26 - Bagratica | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRhNPq88JF8u0gs33wHht%252Ffooter-26.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02873542-6e14-458d-b5d7-dcde29971125&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9773ca10&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FjKCSbP48sARHCB4XOzXa%252Ffooter-26-menu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5772ebc-cad5-46b8-9b5d-4537256bd024&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a54c4fbc&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

*   The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F14LkLd2ByjDzPjmA7aBJ%252Ffooter-26-newsletter.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd396b1e-3a2f-4512-8d4d-8e42de7e963f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=982b8f7e&sv=2)

*   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons. Enable or swap the position with the newsletter as you prefer.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FoqUTxzFuKrKH9ECjv9Pq%252Ffooter-26-social.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D472a27df-b20c-4e47-aefc-75a49ffaef91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c2466bd&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FWTqd4vCeg8r2APFaz9mp%252Ffooter-1-setting-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b4b426e-83e7-42fd-a3e1-be68fbb23f60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=486960e1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-26-bagratica#upload-settings-for-footer)

Upload Settings For Footer


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

► To setup Footer Home 22 - Eyes Wears, you need to add the **Newsletter** and **Footer 01** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 01** section to add.

# How To Set Up Product Property By Metafields? | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F6Fk0GeROhqpBnAGB7hts%252Fproduct-property-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2093a670-b6dc-4b42-ad75-ca131d94f405&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12c2bbce&sv=2)

There are 2 ways to set up: **By Product Metafields** and **By Variant Metafields**

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#by-product-metafields)

**By Product Metafields**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#id-01-add-a-new-product-metafield)

**01: Add a new Product Metafield:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FBuFwpBv2o3fPUJiC4H0F%252Fmeta-field.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58a9be46-483a-461d-ba87-7bef16a76dce&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24646a94&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#id-02-insert-the-content-for-product-metafield)

02: Insert the content for Product Metafield:

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the content for "**Property**" field with **JSON format**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fb5lGwvNypDycYZmP84Dg%252Fproduct-property-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc069c416-c83b-4665-91b8-06901eadc8a6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3259cb64&sv=2)

circle-info

You can use Bulk Editor to edit multiple products.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#by-variant-metafields)

**By Variant Metafields**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#id-01-add-a-new-variant-metafield)

**01: Add a new Variant Metafield:**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Variants → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FUmggtOawf8J1vftP4CC8%252Fmeta-field-variant.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd16450d-127a-45dd-ac01-f1333de67be2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=995ed023&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvBY0MNcYnQJ8IxFjn1Uc%252Fproduct-property-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14827746-d4af-4d82-89dd-9717b6734f08&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da656b49&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#id-02-insert-the-content-for-variant-metafield)

02: Insert the content for Variant Metafield:

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  Choose variant to edit.
    
4.  In the **Metafields**, please enter the content for "**Variant Property**" field with **JSON format**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FErmpMChoejEg5uop3uD4%252Fproduct-property-5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9d53f20-438b-4ec2-975f-96876e9f198c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b09178af&sv=2)

[PreviousHow To Set Up Product Description For Each Variant?chevron-left](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-description-for-each-variant)
[NextHow To Set Up Complementary Products?chevron-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-complementary-products)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [By Product Metafields](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#by-product-metafields)

*   [02: Insert the content for Product Metafield:](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#id-02-insert-the-content-for-product-metafield)

*   [02: Insert the content for Variant Metafield:](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-product-property-by-metafields#id-02-insert-the-content-for-variant-metafield)
    

Copy

    Name: Product Property or any name.
    Namespace and key: c_f.property
    Select content type: JSON

Copy

    Sample code:
    
    {
      "Width": "182 cm",
      "Height": "182 cm",
      "Depth": "39 cm",
      "Max. Load/Shelf": "13 kg",
      "Article Number": "703.015.42",
      "Package": "1"
    }

Copy

    Name: Variant Property or any name.
    Namespace and key: c_f.property
    Select content type: JSON

Copy

    Sample Codes:
    
    {
      "Width": "70 cm",
      "Height": "76 cm",
      "Depth": "58 cm",
      "Min. Height": "33 cm",
      "Seat Depth": "48 cm",
      "Seat Height": "45 cm",
      "Gross Weight": "14.53 kg",
      "Package(s)": "1",
      "Item Number": "404.556.49",
      "Color": "Yellow",
      "Frame": "Plywood (poplar), polyurethane 35kg/m³, polyurethane 30kg/m³, steel, epoxy-based powder coating",
      "Fixed seat": "Polyurethane 30kg/m³, polyester wadding, highly elastic polyurethane (cold foam) 35 kg/m³",
      "Loose Pillow": "Highly elastic polyurethane (cold foam) 23 kg/m³, polyester wadding",
      "Legs": "Steel, Epoxy/polyester Powder Coating",
      "Material": "100% polyester",
      "Designer": "BINGSTA",
      "Made in": "Swedish"
    }

# How To Set Up Complementary Products? | Ella Documentation

Using the [Shopify Search & Discoveryarrow-up-right](https://apps.shopify.com/search-and-discovery)
 app, you can choose specific products to display as complementary products in the product information section on your website's product pages.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FUIo9y1YUNlEmvLnQccCO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De52f43d6-62c7-4736-8bb6-7adeae6ca3c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f67ca9&sv=2)

Layout Style Default

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fedjk3ColF4NfaaW4Ndsz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f398a05-e9ee-4a1c-be0b-93c0f4f2f278&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e85bf1ff&sv=2)

Layout Style Custom

Instruction Video

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-complementary-products#complementary-products-block-settings)

Set Up Complementary Products Block

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Apps** -> **Search & Discovery.**
    
2.  Click **View recommendations** button in the **Feature overview** section.
    
3.  Click **Add recommendations** button.
    
4.  Select the main product to show the Complementary Products block in the **Select source product** section.
    
5.  Select complementary products in the **Add complementary products** section.
    
6.  Click **Save**.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FbaMWcofBJzQyP2AJooaT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0b78300-3f0f-4af6-ae88-ee5391a1ad58&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6908682&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/how-to-set-up-complementary-products#customizing-the-appearance-of-complementary-products)

Customizing Complementary Products

1\. From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.

2\. Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.

3\. Choose **Default product** template in the dropdown of editor window to open theme editor of product page.

4\. From **Product information ->** Click **Add block** \-> Choose **Complementary products.**

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FbSefXfLpR5peIAh1rpqG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2af66f7a-eaf8-4fce-9d15-bc1b60d63683&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1338c283&sv=2)

Setting

Description

Heading

Enter the title for the section.

Layout

Select the layout for the items of the product block to be either Grid or List.

Maximum products to show for grid layout

Select the number of visible products for grid layout.

Maximum products to show for list layout

Select the number of visible products for list layout.

Show navigation arrows

Show/Hide the navigation arrows for the slider layout.

Show navigation dots

Show/Hide the dots for the slider layout.

**Product card**

Media fit

Determine of how to display product images

Enable add to cart button

Show/Hide add to cart button on each product item.

**Block padding**

Top padding

Determine the top spacing of the section.

Bottom padding

Determine the bottom spacing of the section.

3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.

Upload Settings For Footer


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 27 - Men Fashion 02, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-27-men-fashion-02#preset-for-footer-home-27-men-fashion-02)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRPtqwgG6ABSZWhqME4z6%252Ffooter-group-edit.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d3b1071-06c8-4f29-b2cb-cf36a84c9363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9f9ffab&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvHQLpfLSzhMz3HFSkXYS%252Ffooter-10-setting-footer-bottom.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68f2d209-1fc4-4280-bf30-b1981be75f18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a3d153c&sv=2)

# Home 33 - Coffee Shop | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOixC2j6KWSku7AcZnzMJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da45ba2f4-f22b-4ce5-8d9f-f32a7d72d1c3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7ba997c&sv=2)

[Home 33 - Coffee Shoparrow-up-right](https://new-ella.myshopify.com/?preview_theme_id=130564915298)

► To set up the footer for **Home 33 - Coffee Shop**, you need to add the **Footer 01** section to the **Footer Group**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **Footer Group ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Footer 01** section.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOtniJFv4XHWoIGuSLPwm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf235df9-9932-43cf-85b0-b39454822240&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6220fd7&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 01** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 3. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FZ0PNjQsu17IbqOcEbewd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6540eea-c474-4487-b332-53ce14cdd096&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=378ebe29&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FIDhI7Z8e22q5YLNXIfOq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df940b4d3-45e8-4cf1-80ea-45a1c7faa901&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=159337&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F8EKU3uoIlpp09lXBYjFc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De368219d-52bc-4539-890b-8b0e3edaeaea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88bb27da&sv=2)

1.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    

The settings are for the block width, heading, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FvVy6UilrqQAcrE0i3vPr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D660bb5ff-9fbb-4767-a8ff-96e98b87a166&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=711e6b3b&sv=2)

# Home 23 - Plant+ Garden | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FG3cyhSTaunwmapGNS20G%252Ffooter-23.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b8bbd7d-a86d-4662-9db8-b7ee0de5557f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=744e7fe2&sv=2)

[Home 23 - Plant+ Gardenarrow-up-right](https://new-ella-demo-11.myshopify.com/?fts=0&preview_theme_id=124314517555)

► To setup Footer Home 23 - Plant+ Garden, you need to add the **Newsletter** and **Footer 07** sections to the **FOOTER GROUP**.

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to Online **Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  At the **FOOTER GROUP ->** click **+** **Add section**.
    
4.  Search and select **Newsletter** section.
    
5.  Same for **Footer 07** section to add.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FyDpC3DDh6lyO8SB1D71u%252Ffooter-21-add-section.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaeee6ab-1795-44c5-aee0-d5b20ec51d9d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=333c0947&sv=2)

► In the **Newsletter** section settings. Add or adjust **Newsletter** block as your need:

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FafOYVaUQPWoBs5WtpiDE%252Ffooter-21-newsletter.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f562ffb-5d1c-4d3c-b6af-b8b7c7ec7859&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a3f460&sv=2)

► In the **Footer 07** section settings. Add or adjust these blocks as your need:

1.  **Text** block: Limit 1. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    
2.  **Menu** block: Limit 3. The settings are for the block width, title, and menu selection for menu.
    
3.  **Newsletter** block: Limit 1.
    
    *   The settings are for the block width, title, description, button text along with their colors, spacing, background color.
        
    *   At the bottom half of the settings, there are also settings for Social Media icons.
        
    *   The subtext (description) will lay on top of the title.
        
    *   And the whole block will be aligned to a different direction of other blocks.
        
    *   If other blocks are to the left of the section, the newsletter block will be aligned to the right.
        
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F4hUP71oxcIqEfGkzNsYq%252Ffooter-7-setting-1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd974c292-82f2-4aaf-b581-40f163715369&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50538791&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FMU1KuskiBxA53thlPY2U%252Ffooter-7-setting-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D154e2074-19c6-467a-80bd-134340718f42&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa8855e7&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FDcF4Ikc4zAGcbdOb7Dmn%252Ffooter-21-bottom.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5519bc93-13eb-48f0-8f5c-6fbcf3bcbc01&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=514bb311&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FivYP9n2arBsTUC2hTXAJ%252Ffooter-21-payment.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D871bd319-308a-4ff3-b1b4-1bbbfee299de&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce50b58a&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FQuRPTtJVyI5UfP9C13ir%252Ffooter-31-social.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4bf67c32-68fd-4969-bdf7-a1a4bd7ab6ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b463df9&sv=2)

1.  **Text** block: Limit 2. The block allows you to upload logo image, address, phone and emails with icons.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F0nvAoDtlJ19swjgHvvML%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc92b29c-5b0c-4ef4-95f4-35f062eb615a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=463ad22f&sv=2)

1.  **Menu** block: Limit 4. The settings are for the block width, heading, and menu selection for menu.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FSA3FtHjaAN2EgYuZfROW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd1c3fdb-8dbc-4764-a065-0598560754e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=651d494a&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F9v7qjhZ2tmlVjmd0Lnzz%252Ffooter-31-menu-2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3433203-542f-40f6-975d-c71bb6e2d98b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99b2ec14&sv=2)

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F2ONNX2GVfTUnzrdCZS3M%252Ffooter-31-menu-3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf181526-c080-47d2-9abb-326b86a9c5a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8d77d5cb&sv=2)

1.  **Footer Bottom** block: Limit 1. The settings are for copyright and payment methods with their positions choice.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fuho61A0M5jkrWGdjCQxQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6e0d7d5-892a-45b1-9967-0ae3cc0f4b25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8f67703&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-31-hair-wigs#upload-settings-for-footer)

Upload Settings For Footer


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up data for Footer Home 31 - Hair Wigs, please follow below instruction:

1.  Click the [file to downloadarrow-up-right](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-31-hair-wigs#preset-for-home-31-hair-wigs)
     the corresponding _"json"_ of the layout you want to open the data on a new tab.
    
2.  **SELECT ALL** and **COPY**.
    
3.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Themes** **\->** **Actions** **\->** **Edit Code.**
    
4.  Find folder **Sections** **\->** Open file **footer-group.json** **\->** **SELECT ALL** and **DELETE** then **PASTE** the copied preset from the external file.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FGf0d8QTWmgo31JyagSnH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3206bcde-9917-4c18-9ea9-033ddd5c1d3d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfbfca7d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/footer/footer-layout/home-31-hair-wigs#preset-for-home-31-hair-wigs)

# Size Chart | Ella Documentation

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252Fb39AeBnpz5hGBIe7x8EN%252F141.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81006810-c76b-442d-b7c1-c245aed8b8c3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17fc62ea&sv=2)

circle-info

Ella offers 5 ways to show the Size chart:

*   [By Product Type](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-product-type)
    
*   [By Product Vendor](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-product-vendor)
    
*   [By Metafield](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-metafield)
    
*   [By Custom Image](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-custom-image)
    
*   [By Custom Page](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-custom-page)
    

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-product-type)

By Product Type


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Products** from the dropdown window.
    
4.  On **Product information** \-> add **Perks** block (if not already added).
    
5.  On **Perks** block scroll down to **Size chart** and choose **Size chart type** as **Product type.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FuCn2ce4BeTIz0zsr3i5I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b8fa535-2244-4063-9124-846f2401ef85&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3077f76&sv=2)

circle-info

Upload image with the same name as the product-type-sizechart. You need to go to Settings --> Files upload images here.

Naming convention: lower cap and use "-" to replace white space. For example: with the product type "Loremous Comodous" the image name will be loremous-comodous-sizechart.jpg or loremous-comodous-sizechart.png

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-product-vendor)

By Product Vendor


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Products** from the dropdown window.
    
4.  Click **Product information** \-> add **Perks** block (if not already added).
    
5.  On **Perks** block scroll down to **Size chart** and choose **Size chart type** as **Product vendor.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252F07N0tE4zsiC9CDOy5XMv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4e1bd22-c908-4225-ae11-03d476241336&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e3b33b3&sv=2)

circle-info

Upload image with the same name as the product-vendor-sizechart.

To get the image URL, please upload the image in **Content** **\->** **Files**. Then copy the link. You can refer to [this linkarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/shopify-admin/productivity-tools/file-uploads)
.

Naming convention: lower cap and use "-" to replace white space. For example: with the product vendor "Loremous Comodous" the image name will be loremous-comodous-sizechart.jpg or loremous-comodous-sizechart.png

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-metafield)

By Metafield


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Products** from the dropdown window.
    
4.  Click **Product information** \-> add **Perks** block (if not already added).
    
5.  On **Perks** block scroll down to **Size chart** and choose **Size chart type** as **Product metafield.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FZchPQhoxmWiBEqNPvKAF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3548000f-bd8c-41c6-a55e-4db9831a2d0c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb625188&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#how-to-add-new-metafields)

H**ow to add new Metafields?**

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Settings** -> **Custom data**.
    
2.  Click **Products → Add Definition.**
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FPTqNndRguDzb15QPCqT0%252Fmeta-field.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904657ee-9381-4d21-a258-56b1c8d7c2bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56c7e2e9&sv=2)

1.  Please enter correct **Namespace and Key** as we noted below.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FFkwxlfBWyvydJWzVAX3G%252Fsizechart-3.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da81dd1e5-7f11-4e52-83e9-e21179a28d87&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a64390c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#how-to-insert-content-for-product-metafields)

How to insert content for Product Metafields?

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Products -> All products**.
    
2.  Find and choose the product that you want to edit.
    
3.  In the **Metafields**, please insert image url in the "**Size Chart**" field.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FRbKaPyuVBj6qVOLXSf6u%252Fsizechart-4.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D12c081f1-625c-41bb-af9a-0d21a75ae194&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da55db4&sv=2)

circle-info

To get the image URL, please upload the image in **Content** **\->** **Files**. Then copy the link. You can refer to [this linkarrow-up-right](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/shopify-admin/productivity-tools/file-uploads)
.

circle-info

You can use Bulk Editor to edit multiple products.

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-custom-image)

By Custom Image


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Products** from the dropdown window.
    
4.  Click **Product information** \-> add **Perks** block (if not already added).
    
5.  On **Perks** block scroll down to **Size chart** and choose **Size chart type** as **Custom image** to apply the size chart for all products**.**
    
6.  Upload the size chart image for all products.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FtyjdS5p2swtLTRuNBLbI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3474b300-40ea-4834-b4eb-49722e314164&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91db98d4&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/product-page/product-information/size-chart#by-custom-page)

By Custom Page


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  From your Shopify admin, go to **Online Store** -> **Themes**.
    
2.  Find the theme that you want to edit, and then click **Customize**.
    
3.  Choose **Products** from the dropdown window.
    
4.  Click **Product information** \-> add **Perks** block (if not already added).
    
5.  On **Perks** block scroll down to **Size chart** and choose **Size chart type** as **Custom page.**
    
6.  At "**Custom page**" select the page that you want to display its content on the size chart popup.
    

![](https://halosoft.gitbook.io/ella-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3284033180-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fag3h7ZduRGWlquTgGUHi%252Fuploads%252FOUy1cpFgQ6pMzrylhsdy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D476967d1-902f-44c2-9ac0-226b7ba83db3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=61170540&sv=2)
